As for the Hengjiang and Liji two ships, the damage was minor, and they can be used after slight repairs. (15th)

Siamese Rice to Be Exclusively Sold by Government 82

Major Impact on Food Supply in Shantou, Hong Kong, and Guangzhou

Shantou News: The people of southern China rely on rice as their staple food, but rice production is quite low, so most of the rice each year depends on imports from other ports. According to a survey by the Social Affairs Section of the Shantou Municipal Government in the 18th year of the Republic, the amount of rice imported from other ports in one year is as follows:

Rice from Singapore: 5,824 dan

Rice from Annam (Saigon): 17,834 dan

Siamese rice via Hong Kong: 253,726 dan

Siamese rice: 783,760 dan

Wuhu rice: 806,302 dan

Rangoon rice: 291,436 dan

In total, about one million dan or more of Siamese rice are sold to Shantou each year. At the current market price, each dan (100 catties) costs 9.6 silver dollars, so the value is about ten million yuan.

Siam is located in Nanyang and has close ties with our country. Since the Qing Dynasty, the government authorities have often overlooked Siam because it is a small country. Last year, there were many calls to sign a commercial treaty with Siam, which attracted great attention from the people of Chaoshan. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent personnel to investigate the number of overseas Chinese in Siam so that consulates could be established after the Sino-Siamese commercial treaty was concluded. According to the report from the investigating committee returning to Beijing last winter, the population of Siam is approximately 9,520,000, including 3,800,000 Sino-Siamese mixed-race people, 3,650,000 Lao people, 500,000 pure Chinese people, 450,000 Khmer people, 400,000 Malay people, 120,000 Mongol and Karen people, and 60,000 Saba aborigines. The above population numbers are based on the Siamese government's survey. The Siamese government is silent about the power of the overseas Chinese, so it only mentions that there are 500,000 adult male overseas Chinese in Bangkok, Siam (those who have paid their personal tax). Most of the locally born children and family members are not included. According to the statistics of Siamese researcher Mr. Parnai Cheng (a Siamese priest), there are 1.5 million overseas Chinese in Siam. According to the German Milner's Universal Gazetteer, there are 2.5 to 3 million overseas Chinese in Siam. I traveled to Bangkok ten years ago and saw that the city was full of Chinese people, and the Chaozhou dialect had become the common language in Siamese cities. Chaozhou people occupy an important position in the agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors of Siam. Shantou has a Siamese Chamber of Commerce, which is the central hub for overseas Chinese trade. Siam's exports are dominated by timber and white rice. Timber for shipbuilding around the world has long been nationalized for official sale. White rice is exported to southern China and Japan. Large-scale rice mills are all in the hands of our Chinese people. This spring, Chaoshan rice merchants received letters from Siamese joint ventures stating that the Siamese government has decided to nationalize the export of rice, and Chinese rice mills will be forced to close down. This matter has a great impact on the food supply of southern China, and our countrymen should pay close attention to it.

New Rural Village Projects in Jiangsu Agricultural Department 83

Huangxu Has Roughly Taken Shape; Provincial Government Approves Allocation of 1,000 Yuan in Subsidies

In order to improve rural areas throughout the province, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines has designated five locations for model new rural villages: the Salt Reclamation Area, Chunhua Town, Changgou Village, Shijia墩, and Xinfeng District (now renamed Huangxu District). These five locations were to be subsidized as part of the 18th-year budget, but because of financial constraints in the provincial treasury, the Salt Reclamation Area, Chunhua Town, and Changgou Village were not started, and subsidies for the Shijia墩 new rural village were temporarily suspended. However, since Huangxu is near the provincial capital, in order to demonstrate success, the Zhenjiang County Huangxu Rural Improvement Experimental Zone Committee was organized in October of last year and has been responsible for handling the project. Progress has been uninterrupted so far. Major works in the district, such as the construction of the Xin-Huang highway, surveying the water level, renovating the assembly hall, expanding the people's night school, setting up a public reading room and a public sports field, compiling household registration for villagers, improving local sanitation, and reclaiming wasteland for planting mulberry trees and afforestation, have roughly taken shape. However, the original budget for the district was only 2,000 yuan, which has already been fully received. Currently, various projects urgently require funds. The budget for this year still requires 1,000 silver dollars. In order to maintain the district's project, the Department of Agriculture and Mines specifically proposed to the provincial government that 1,000 yuan be misappropriated from other new rural village subsidies. An order was issued to the Finance Department to release the funds early to facilitate progress, which has been approved by the Provincial Government Committee.

Disturbance in Linhai County, Zhejiang Province, Has Been Resolved 84

The Zhejiang Provincial Government previously received a telegram from Linhai County Magistrate Hou Changling reporting that bandit Wang Xiaojian and others in Guankeng Village in the southern part of the county were opposing land surveying and reporting, and after shooting and killing a team leader and two soldiers of the Naraixi Village Defense Corps, gathered more than 300 bandits and occupied Guankeng Village and Shanggan Shamen and other places. The county magistrate led a team to suppress the bandits twice, but failed to eliminate them due to the treacherous terrain, and requested that the provincial army be sent to suppress them. After receiving the telegram, the provincial government, in addition to ordering the county magistrate to take proper precautions, specifically telegraphed Zhu Mingtao, commander of the 5th Regiment of the Haimen Security Corps, to quickly lead a team to Linhai to suppress the bandits and investigate and handle the lead offenders. Commander Zhu has now led a battalion of infantry and a machine gun company from Haimen to Linhai to suppress the bandits. A telegram has already been sent to the province reporting that local order has been restored. Bandit leader Wang Xiaojian is on the run and is currently being tracked down for punishment.

Dangerous Signs for the Future of Food Supply in Zhejiang Province 85

Government Rice for Equalization of Prices Looted En Route; Seven People Died in Hangzhou in One Day

Due to excessive disasters in various counties of Zhejiang Province and a lack of food for the people, the local situation is intermittently unstable. The provincial government approved the Civil Affairs Department's plan to borrow funds to purchase rice to implement equalization of prices, and members were dispatched by the Chamber of Commerce to purchase rice from Hunan, Anhui, and other provinces. However, after three or four months, the rice has still not been transported. The food supply for the severely affected counties relies entirely on the rice provided by the Jisheng Association and the Relief Affairs Association. Fortunately, 3,000 piculs of government rice purchased by the province in Jiangsu has already been shipped, but a rice looting incident occurred en route. Previously, the provincial government ordered the special service company of the 2nd Regiment of the Changxing Security Corps to send troops to protect the government rice. When the rice passed through Lushan, about 500 poor people gathered to riot. Lin Xishi, the officer of the company, immediately implemented suppression, but the rice had already been forcefully looted by the poor people. Seven or eight principal offenders, including Zhou Wencai, Lin Bao Rong, and Guo Jin Song, were arrested on the spot and sent to the 2nd Regiment for interrogation. After persuasion, the rest each took rice and dispersed. The rice has now been transported past Shiqiao and will arrive in Hangzhou in a few days. However, 3,000 piculs will be distributed to various counties for equalization of prices, so each county will receive very little. It will take time to wait for funds to be transferred and re-purchased, and the food problem cannot be resolved. The local future is precarious. For example, Lu Ayou, a resident outside Wangjiangmen in Hangzhou, his wife, and their two sons, committed suicide by hanging because rice was expensive and food was difficult to find. Sun Defa, who lived in Houjie Street, Zhakou, also hanged himself with his mother due to poverty and illness. In addition, an old woman named Xiao, who lived in 200 rooms on Putisi Road in the new market, also committed suicide because rice was expensive. Statistics show that seven people died in one day due to the high price of rice. The dangerous signs of the food situation can be seen generally. (18th)

Hangzhou Express News 86

The Construction Department plans to summon construction personnel from all counties in the province to Hangzhou to discuss local construction projects in their respective counties, covering transportation, agriculture, mining, industry, commerce, water conservancy, as well as railways, highways, telecommunications, and other areas.

The Finance and Construction Departments, upon receiving a dispatch from the provincial government regarding a request from the Hangzhou silk industry for tax reduction or exemption, have had Construction Department Secretary Huo Baoshu and Finance Department Secretary-General Gu Guiyu engage in substantive discussions. It is reported that Hangzhou factories require raw silk, and each 80 catties is subject to an additional Shanghai tax of 3.2 yuan, while each case of artificial silk is subject to an additional Shanghai tax of 13 yuan. Complete exemption of both items is unlikely to achieve the desired outcome, but a reasonable reduction is hoped for.

The Hangzhou General Chamber of Commerce has borrowed commercial funds to procure rice at stable prices. Tang Yongfu has been dispatched to Shanghai to order 5,000 piculs of Saigon rice. This rice is expected to be shipped to Hangzhou in batches soon. It is reported that the Civil Affairs Department has decided to allocate 2,000 piculs of rice and issue a document to the Three Granaries Committee to subsidize sales at stable prices. The remaining 3,000 piculs will be distributed to rice merchants for sale at affordable prices.

The Hangzhou Municipal and County Rice Price Assessment Committee held its 12th temporary meeting yesterday. The matters discussed were: (1) A proposal to sell grades of rice from pawnshops without additional screening and based directly on their original quality. It was decided that screening should continue as before, and the quality grades of rice from pawnshops would temporarily remain as they were, with further discussion to be postponed. (2)

Assessing rice prices: It was decided that, starting from the 19th, the price of top-grade rice, medium-grade rice, as well as steamed glutinous rice and late-season indica rice, would each increase by 40 cents per picul. Medium-to-lower-grade rice would increase by 20 cents. Glutinous rice prices would remain the same. To safeguard the interests of the poor, the prices of entry-level rice and rice for the common people would not be allowed to increase. (18th)

Songjiang 88

Minutes of the County Government Meeting: The County Government held its 49th meeting yesterday, with Chairman Jin of the County Government presiding. (1) Regarding the boats of the Shaoxing guild in this port, which charge varying prices to out-of-town passengers who hire them, it was proposed that this practice should be banned to benefit travelers. It was decided that fixed prices should be established for all types of boats. The County Magistrate should instruct the Construction Bureau to conduct a detailed investigation and draft regulations and a price list for review at a meeting. (2) Regarding the many bridge reconstructions within the First District, including those completed, unfinished, in progress, or planned, the question was raised whether the Construction Bureau should inspect and review them to ensure the quality of the projects. It was decided that the reconstruction of bridges is an important matter. Completed bridges should be reported by the First District Office to the County Government and then forwarded to the Construction Bureau for inspection. For bridges in progress or planned, the names of the bridges and their plans should be submitted to the County Government and then forwarded to the Construction Bureau for review before construction begins. (3) Regarding the proposed reconstruction of the Puzhao Temple Bridge, which connects to the main street and sees heavy pedestrian and vehicular traffic, and whether the Construction Bureau should prepare the plans before construction begins, it was decided to approve the proposal and instruct the Construction Bureau and the First District Office to implement it accordingly.

Fengxian 89

Aftermath of the Robbery at Xuli Bridge: Following the robbery at Xuli Bridge, fortunately, reinforcements from Nanqiao arrived, and the merchants were not affected. Magistrate Hong led police to the town that night to handle the aftermath. All the deceased Police Officer Chen and merchant Gao Xiang, who was killed by a stray bullet, have been separately collected and coffined. However, the two seriously injured policemen were escorted back and claimed that the hospital refused to treat them due to excessive blood loss. After repeated negotiations, the hospital reluctantly agreed. Surgery is currently underway, and if the bullets can be removed without complications, it may be possible to save them. The cost is reportedly quite high, and the two heads of the county bureau are temporarily providing assistance. As for the pursuit of the perpetrators, the county government held an emergency meeting last night based on intelligence, and it is expected that a breakthrough will be made soon. Regarding town defense, the police station has lost all its firearms, so yesterday, two platoons of the county police force were dispatched to reinforce the defense. The original police force in various locations, which was already thin, has also been supplemented by two squads of the yet-to-be-established temporary police force, dispatched by the county on a strict schedule to increase strength.

Medical and Pharmaceutical Commemoration Meeting: Four groups, including the Chinese Medicine Association and the Commercial Association Pharmaceutical Society, have been preparing for the March 17th Medical and Pharmaceutical Struggle Commemoration for a long time. All slogans, declarations, and commemoration methods were prepared and printed in advance according to the regulations of the Shanghai General Association. At 1:00 PM today (the 17th), comrades from both the medical and pharmaceutical fields were gathered at the public square in Nanqiao to hold a meeting. The special commissioner of the county party headquarters attended to provide guidance. The meeting concluded at 5:00 PM with a group photo.

Suzhou 90

Lake Bandits Rampant, Recruiting Boatmen: After the Yang Santai Temple on the shores of Yangcheng Lake, where the border of Suzhou and Kunshan meets, was occupied by more than 300 lake bandits, the bandits have become increasingly rampant. Not only are they robbing in nearby villages, but the bandits even sent out members to recruit 30 boatmen, distributing rations to them. The other day (the 15th), Wang Sanxuan, a villager from Hudian Township outside the West Gate of Changshu, and his son Xingxing and cousin Wang Shinu, sailed to Suzhou to purchase seedlings and fertilizer. As they passed the area, they were stopped by the bandits, who took Wang Sanxuan away and declared that they were under the orders of Old Woman Guo to recruit boatmen. Shinu, seeing his brother taken away by the bandits, returned to Changshu to report to the county government for pursuit. The Anti-Bandit Army: The 13th Brigade of the Anti-Bandit Army General Headquarters, dispatched from Bengbu, arrived in Suzhou on the evening of the 17th and stationed at the West Garden Jietang Temple. The First Battalion of the 25th Regiment hired boats yesterday morning to proceed to Wujiang. The regimental headquarters is stationed at the Chenghuang Temple in Wujiang. Today (the 19th), they will be stationed in Pingwang North and other places. Commander Hu believes that only Hengjing and the East and West Mountains of Taihu Lake can concentrate troops. If he intends to distribute troops to various villages, the troop strength is still insufficient, so a comprehensive plan is still needed.

The Death Sentence for 171 Bandit Leaders and Accomplices: Taihu bandit leader Zhu Yubo was arrested in Shanghai last November and brought to Suzhou for interrogation. The local court sentenced him to death on the 17th, along with 171 accomplices. The main points of the verdict are as follows: For the crime of collectively gathering in the mountains and resisting government troops, he is sentenced to death and deprived of civil rights indefinitely. For the six counts of jointly committing robbery and intentionally killing people, he is sentenced to death and deprived of civil rights indefinitely for each count. For the 94 counts of jointly committing robbery while holding firearms, engaging in large-scale robbery, robbery on the sea, and resisting government troops, he is sentenced to death and deprived of civil rights indefinitely for each count. For the 74 counts of kidnapping for ransom, he is sentenced to death and deprived of civil rights indefinitely for each count. He shall be executed and deprived of civil rights indefinitely. Once the appeal is approved, the sentence must be carried out according to law.

The Verdict in the Case of the Patrol Officer Neglecting His Duty: Gu Shurong, the former patrol officer of the Wushenjing Public Security Substation, was sentenced to seven years and six months in prison by the Wuxian Local Court for using private torture that resulted in the death of a petty thief named Sun Da Kui. The court sent personnel to the countryside to conduct an examination, which confirmed the facts. Gu was brought to court for trial. Gu did not accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court. The second instance upheld the original verdict. Gu still refused to accept it and appealed to the Supreme Court, which sent the case back to the High Court for retrial. The verdict was announced yesterday, overturning the original sentence and reducing it to four years and six months of imprisonment.

The Case of the Robbery at the Head of the Security Corps' House Solved: Zhang Pu, the head of the Xukou Township Security Corps in the Mudu District of the county, had his house robbed by five bandits on the 13th. The bandits fled in different directions after obtaining the stolen goods. The Second District Seventh Squad of the resident Mudu Water Police arrested Tian A-Xi, the principal offender, in Mudu Town. After interrogation by Captain Li, he confessed without denial and also implicated accomplices Shi A-Gui and Wu A-Da. The squad then captured Shi A-Gui, who also confessed. Later, a suspect named Fang Guifu was apprehended and sent to the Second District of Wuxi for processing on the 17th.

Wuxi 91

The County Government Examines the Body of a Child: It was discovered that there was the body of a wounded boy inside the Shiqiaobang of Huai Township in the county. Liu Chunlan, the leader of the First Squad of the First Company of the resident County Police Team, investigated and found three suspects, Yang A-Da and others. Yesterday, it was learned that County Government Adjudicator Yu, accompanied by Examiner Shen, took a motorboat to the countryside to conduct a legal examination. The examination determined that the deceased boy was about eleven or twelve years old and had been severely beaten with an iron instrument and buried alive. After the examination, as no family members of the deceased came to claim the body, the local bailiff was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial and affix a seal to the altar. Mr. Yu and others then returned to the city by car. As for the suspects Yang A-Da and others, after interrogation by Squad Leader Liu yesterday, it was determined that they were not involved, and they were released on bail separately.

Water Police Seize Privately Transported Rice Boats: There is not much rice stored in this county, and sources from various places are scarce. However, unscrupulous merchants, disregarding the people's food supply, are transporting large quantities of rice out of the county, causing rice prices to rise daily, causing panic among ordinary people. However, the Zhou Yuchang Rice Shop outside the South Gate of Huangnifeng secretly loaded about 100 stones of white rice onto a boat to transport it to Changxing, Zhejiang Province. Yesterday, it was seized by the squadron leader of the Third Platoon of the Sixth Team of the Second District of the Waterfront Provincial Public Security Team, stationed in Wuxi, Ji Zaiyang, and Officer Li, at Daxuankou. They were immediately brought into the city and transferred to the district headquarters. District Chief Mao interrogated the boatman Wang Jinguai, who claimed that the rice was being transported to Zhejiang Province and that he had a passport from the Construction Committee of the National Government. District Chief Mao, based on the confession, telegraphed the Civil Affairs Department for instructions on how to handle the matter. Late-Night Tragedy of Two Murders by Gunfire: Yang Xianyi, a resident of No. 23 Sibao Alley outside the North Gate of this county, was known as a famous "swallow's nest" for selling opium. At around 1:00 PM yesterday afternoon, five people dressed in soldiers' uniforms and speaking in a foreign accent suddenly came to Yang Xianyi's house, demanding money to smoke opium, pestering him endlessly. Yang politely refused, and the men left resentfully. Unexpectedly, at 9:45 PM, just after the Yang family finished dinner, they suddenly heard someone knocking urgently on the back door (the door used for people to enter and exit when selling opium). Xianyi thought it was an opium addict and personally opened the door. He caught a glimpse of six people dressed in uniforms resembling deserters. Two of them carried Mauser pistols, and four held handguns. The deserters entered the door and, without asking any questions, swept the room with the Mauser pistols. Yang Xianyi's eldest son, Yang Quanjin (30 years old), and opium servant Wu Rinsheng (62 years old, from Tianshangsi, Shangshi) were instantly shot and fell to the ground, dead. The six deserters immediately fled towards Shuxiang Lane. Yang Quanjin, who died tragically, was shot four times, and opium servant Wu Rinsheng was shot once, both in vital areas. After the incident, the Public Security Bureau of the county government dispatched detectives to search for the murderers, but they could not be found. At 11:00 PM that night, Yang Xianyi, accompanied by the local bailiff Wu Jiahe, went to the county government to report the incident for an examination. The county government, considering the severity of the case, immediately sent Adjudicator Yu, accompanied by Examiner Shen, to the scene to conduct an examination. The examination confirmed that Yang Quanjin and Wu Rinsheng had both died from gunshot wounds before death. The bodies were coffined by the Yang family, and a receipt was issued for the coffin. They then returned to the county government.

Changzhou 92

Robbery and Assault at Hutang Bridge: On the evening of the 17th, at around 8:00 PM, Xu Heshang Zhuang Shunlin and others from Shitoutou Village, Hutang Bridge, outside the South Gate of Wu County, were stopped by three robbers who robbed them of dozens of silver dollars. At this time, Chen Hongsheng, a rickshaw puller, happened to be passing by and saw the robbery. He shouted loudly, and the robbers opened fire, hitting him in the waist. He was seriously injured and taken to the hospital for treatment, and his life may be in danger.

Commemoration Meeting of the Medical and Pharmaceutical Branch: The Preparatory Office of the Wujin County Branch of the National Medical and Pharmaceutical General Association held a commemoration meeting at the Chamber of Commerce on March 17th, the anniversary of the founding of the General Association. Several hundred people attended. After the meeting, it was decided to raise construction funds, with medical members contributing one yuan each and pharmaceutical members contributing two yuan per store. The meeting also appointed four representatives to attend the annual general meeting of the General Association: Tu Boyuan, Zhu Lvan, Li Diyun, and Wu Jifu. A group photo was then taken, and the meeting adjourned.

Jiangyin 93

Extortion by Bandits for Enclosure Fields: Huang Zhu Xian of Dingshu Township, Sixth District, was abducted by bandits in Weicun, Wujin, the other day. His clothes were stripped off, but he was rescued by the anti-smuggling team. Zhu Xian was also searched by bandits for more than 1,000 yuan of enclosure field money and was forced to write an IOU for 3,000 yuan in the Land Temple of Weicun, with a deadline of 500 days to pay. Huang has reported to the county for investigation.

Local Funds Department Borrows Money to Survive: The Local Funds Department is in dire financial straits. Deputy Directors Xia Sunhu and others have resigned their posts. The County Party Department is starting its reorganization work and needs 400 yuan for operating expenses. The custodian of the committee, Xu Jiangye, has handed over all funds received during the custody period to conclude his duties, requiring 800 yuan. The second term of the District Chief Training Institute is nearing graduation, and subsidies of 150 yuan are needed. These three funds are urgently needed, so the department has borrowed 1,000 yuan from Chengfengzhuang to meet the immediate need, with the Finance Bureau providing a guarantee.

Local Finances in Dire Straits: Finance Bureau Director Dai Yuandu is unable to meet the demands of various agencies because revenue from taxes is meager and insufficient to cover expenses. The local funds under the grain transport item have not been collected, amounting to about 150,000 yuan. It is now proposed to follow the precedent of borrowing money during the military era, gathering leaders of various legal entities, as well as wealthy households and manufacturers, to jointly allocate and borrow 40,000 yuan for the immediate need. At the same time, regulations will be drafted to request the Finance Department to issue local bonds of 100,000 yuan, with the local fees under the grain transport item that have not been collected over the years as collateral. The local bonds will be used to repay various short-term loans, and the remainder will be used to cover the monthly shortfall. Once the original funds are collected, they will be repaid in succession. Yesterday (the 17th), it was submitted to the county for approval.

Zhenjiang 94

Civil Affairs Department Releases Prisoners: The Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department previously detained Ren Tiemei, a suspect in the Xiaoxian rebellion, and Wu Shaonian, Ma Zishu, Xiang Weishan, Zhang Lianchen, Wang Deen, Xu Huairen, Sun Ensong, and Liu Qingyi, who were involved in smuggling opium. Director Miao believed that he should conclude all unresolved cases as the new director was about to arrive in Zhenjiang to take over, so he separately interrogated and released the nine individuals. The only remaining prisoner in the department is one whose case is more serious and cannot be released hastily.

Yangzhou 95

Implementing Reductions in Various Sub-Bureaus and Offices: The original structure of the Public Security Bureaus in this county is inconsistent with the current system. Last year, the county government submitted a request to the Civil Affairs Department to establish one sub-bureau per autonomous region, with four substations in addition to the sub-bureaus in the urban and rural areas, and to abolish all township substations. At that time, due to winter defense, people in various places requested a postponement. Now that winter defense has passed, it is necessary to implement the plan. It is reported that County Magistrate Chen has already compiled a budget and submitted it to the Civil Affairs Department for approval, planning to implement the reductions separately starting from April 1st.

News of Gathering to Seek Revenge: At Hai hour on the 16th, more than a dozen people in short clothing suddenly barged into the home of Wang Yongqing in Zuoxiang, each wielding weapons such as iron rulers. The family thought it was a robbery and tried to hide. Unexpectedly, the thugs went straight into Wang's bedroom, dragged Wang from the bed, beat him severely, leaving him covered in wounds, and threw him to the ground before scattering. After the incident, it was found that two gold rings were lost, but nothing else was missing.

Strange News of a Woman in Labor Possessed by a Demon: Since last year, there have been more than a dozen women who have died after childbirth due to going mad. Unexpectedly, at 10:00 PM last night (the 16th), the eldest daughter-in-law of Cao Wenkui, a clerk in the county government (living on West Street), had a difficult labor. She immediately called out that someone was pulling at the corner of her clothes. Soon after, the child was born, and she gestured wildly as if resisting something before dying. However, the baby girl, who was large and healthy, was also a strange event.

Jingjiang 96

Serving as a Pimp for Bandits, Killed by Bandits: There was a person named Yu Wumazi in Jiang'an Township, Rugao County, who had no legitimate occupation. Recently, he suddenly joined the bandit gang and extorted money outside, pocketing the money for himself. The bandits heard about this and held a grudge against him. So, more than a dozen accomplices dragged Yu out of his bed in the middle of the night, cut off both of his ears with a knife, and then shot him through the chest. They left only after he had died.

Bandit Arrested: Liu Xiguang, a bandit from Xilai Town, has now joined the Rugao bandit gang. This time, he returned home and was arrested by Song Huihan, who was appointed to lead the security corps. An accomplice named Bao Liu was also captured. After interrogation by the county government, the two bandits confessed directly.

Nantong 97

Funding Issues for the Industrial Special Police Force: The Tongtai Haiqi Industrial Special Police Force has three major detachments defending the areas where various industrial salt reclamation companies in Jiangbei are located. On the 17th, a committee was held to discuss the issue of raising funds. It was decided that the companies in the stationed area would temporarily raise funds separately. The case of increasing the pay for the Second Detachment has not yet been resolved.

Distribution of Duties by the County Reorganization Committee: The Nantong County Reorganization Committee distributed duties on the 17th. The results of the voting were: He Jiyun as the Standing Committee Member and Minister of Organization, Lin Tie as the Minister of Training, Wu Jianzhang as the Minister of Publicity, Cai Guohua as the Minister of Popular Education, and Chen Jin as the Standing Committee Member of the Popular Education Association.

Riverbank Collapse, Requesting Provincial Relief: The riverbank in the southwest of Tong County has been collapsing more and more severely recently. The Yaogang Dike bank is rushing to complete the rescue project, but the high tide is surging, and the dike has collapsed again for dozens of feet. The Construction Bureau believes that the cost is huge and the project is complicated, making it difficult to cope with. It has telegraphed the province to send a commissioner to conduct a survey and find a way to provide relief.

Telegraphing the Military Police to Nantong to Suppress Bandits: Due to the rising spring tide, bandit ships are taking the opportunity to invade the coastal area of Nantong. Large groups of local bandits are causing trouble in the eastern townships and inland areas. The county's police force and security corps are weak. The county government and people from all walks of life have telegraphed the provincial defense military police to send teams to Nantong to suppress the bandits. Purchasing and Transporting Foreign Rice to Relieve Famine: Due to the scarce sources of rice in Nantong, panic has arisen. The price of rice has risen to 22 yuan per picul. After consultation among local people from all walks of life, the financial sector is taking the lead in raising more than 200,000 yuan to purchase and transport large quantities of Rangoon rice to Nantong to relieve the rice famine.

Jiashan 98

Lake Bandits Rob Yangjiabin: In recent days, Jiashan County has been in a state of terror due to the rampant lake bandits. The county government received reports of the situation in various districts and requested that the province send teams to suppress the bandits. Two companies of stationed troops arrived one after another. Unexpectedly, the other day, bandits from Yaozhuang Bridge engaged in a fire fight over ticket snatching. Gunshots were heard nearby, and residents were extremely frightened. Afterwards, the victorious gang of bandits drove to Yangjiabin. The villagers and farmers resisted with gunfire, but the bandits landed ashore and surrounded them, confiscating many self-defense firearms and abducting twelve people. They then acted freely, looting countless items, forcibly opening rice groups and emptying them. They even wanted to set fire to the houses, but they were spared after pleading. The patrolling team and water police stationed in Fanxitang, upon hearing the alarm, had already assembled their teams and rushed to encircle and suppress the bandits.

Huzhou 99

All Stores in Dongqiao Village Go on Strike: Zou Yinmei, the village chief of Dongqiao Village near Zhili in the northeast township of this city, opened a Yicheng store in the village. On the afternoon of the 14th, Chapter Patrolman and more than 20 policemen from the Zhili Public Security Bureau suddenly came to the store, each holding a quick gun, claiming to search for opium. Zou Yinmei happened to be out on other business. A certain policeman stabbed Zou's father-in-law, Shen Xinbao, with a gun, injuring his head and waist. The shop assistant Zou Xuanqing was arrested. Later, in front of Ruizhitang, the shopkeeper Zhang Rongqing was also arrested. After this incident, all the stores in the village went on strike starting yesterday morning. The injured Shen Xinbao was taken to the city to have his injuries examined by the court and reported to the county government, awaiting resolution.

Bandits Arrested, Hostage Rescued: Chenxin Temple Town, located at the junction of Lincheng Bridge and Sian in Huzhou, was previously robbed by bandits and several people were kidnapped. The other day, the 8th Company of the 3rd Battalion of the Security Corps captured bandit Li Jinxi in the home of Yi Jinyou (from Henan) in front of the Balimiao Temple near that place, and arrested Yi Jinyou, Yi Jingchang, and three others who were hiding the bandits. They also rescued Zhao Hongshun's three-year-old son. They were all taken to the battalion headquarters for questioning. Li Jinxi confessed that he had worked in the Changxing Coal Mine and joined the bandit gang less than ten days ago. After hearing the confession, the battalion commander prepared a document and escorted them to the city headquarters for processing. The three-year-old hostage has been taken back by Zhao Hongshun after providing a guarantee.

Jiaxing 100

County Education Association Elects Executive Committee Members: The Jiaxing County Education Association elected executive committee members last month, but the election was not conducted according to the regulations. The association was instructed by the department to hold a re-election. It is learned that the association convened a general meeting of all members in Zhongshan Hall yesterday to hold the election. Fang Ying, Chen Jingbo, Chen Zhixiong, Ding Zhenkun, Zhang Wenchang, Shen Wenliang, Niu Jiechun, Ma Shuzi, and Wang Chunong were elected as executive committee members. Ni Jinzhang, Song Dingzhen, and Xu Jue Min were elected as alternate executive committee members.

Hotel Inspection Leads to Arrest of Thieves: Wang Patrolman of the Jiaxing Yuhang Street Substation led police officers to inspect hotels the other night. In room of the Xiuzhou Hotel, they found two suspicious travelers, Wang A-Er and Wang A-Qing. A search was conducted, and various weapons and gold and silver ornaments, as well as pawn tickets, were found on the two men. The witnesses were taken to the bureau together. After detailed interrogation by Director Chen, the two men's statements were inconsistent. Upon inspecting the ornaments, it was found that they all had the markings of Gu Zhengsheng Silver Store on Zhongjie Street in the city, suggesting that they were items from nearby farmhouses. Afterwards, police officer Han Guanrong confirmed that the homes of Tao Dadi, a farmer in Shuangqiao Yisihang, and Shen A-Song, a farmer in Huajiawei, had been robbed ten days ago. The losses were not significant, but the items found matched the items seized from the two men. The victims also identified the two men as the robbers. The two thieves then confessed to colluding to commit the robberies. They have now been sent to the court for trial.

Hangzhou 101

Continuation of New Student Recruitment at the Police Training Institute: The Police Training Institute attached to the Zhejiang Provincial Police Academy has had over 600 student police officers since its opening in December of last year. It is now reported that the school principal, Zhu Jiahua, upon returning to the province from Beijing the other day, immediately inspected the institute and was very satisfied with the results. The first class is about to graduate, and it is planned to recruit several hundred more student police officers for the second class. The institute has submitted a request to the Department of Civil Affairs to instruct the governments of various counties to conduct part of the recruitment examinations on their behalf, with the remainder being recruited in the city. The registration period is from April 1st to May 7th. A recruitment committee has already been formed and is actively preparing.

Scheduled Fundraising for Construction Bonds: The Zhejiang Province has been approved to issue 10 million yuan in construction bonds. The provincial government has decided to solicit bids for printing the bonds. It is reported that the bonds will soon be printed, and the Department of Finance has decided to start fundraising on April 1st. The fundraising will be based on the amount of farmland in each county and will be repaid with priority after the issuance of the six public bonds.

This Year's Highway Construction Plan: The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau yesterday drafted this year's road construction plan: (1) The coastal line, starting from Ningbo, passing through Fenghua, Ninghai, Linhai, Haimen, Huangyan, Yueqing, Yongjia, Ruian, to Pingyang, crossing the border to Fujian, is about 900 li long. (2) The Hangzhou-Jingning line, starting from across the river from Hangzhou, passing through Xiaoshan, Zhuji, Dongyang, Yongkang, Jinyun, Qingshui, to Jingning, reaching Songxi in Fujian, is about 900 li long. (3) The Changshan-Yongjia line, starting from Changshan, passing through Quzhou, Suichang, Songyang, Qingtian, to Yongjia, is about 300 li long. The goal is to complete these within the year.

Urgent Report on the Number of Vagrants: The Zhejiang Department of Civil Affairs, in order to reduce the number of poor people and vagrants in various counties, previously drafted a form and ordered investigations and reports, stipulating that it be carried out in three phases. However, since the order was issued, no county has complied. Yesterday, a strict order was issued to expedite the investigation and submit reports within a limited time, in order to find ways to provide relief.

Saigon Silver Coins to Be Transported to Hangzhou Soon: The Hangzhou Mint has signed a contract with various banks in Shanghai to recoin Saigon silver coins. The first two batches have already been transported to Hangzhou for recoining and then transported to Shanghai. The third batch of 8 million yuan worth of Saigon silver coins is reported to have arrived in Shanghai from India and will be transported to Hangzhou soon. The mint is preparing for the melting and casting process.

Results of the Re-election of the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association: The Zhejiang Provincial Traditional Chinese Medicine Association held its fourth quarterly general meeting, attended by over 300 people. The results of the re-election are as follows: Qiu Jisheng, Tang Shiyan, Hua Zemin, Wang Zemin, Kong Airu, and eleven others were elected as executive committee members, and Ma Shuping and five others were elected as supervisory committee members.

Ningbo 102

Riot During Temple Fair, Patrol Chief Beaten: The Lin Dong district of Yuyao is remote, with strong local customs and widespread superstition. The villagers near Wushan Temple hold a vegetarian fast and worship the gods on the fifteenth day of the second month of the lunar calendar every year. This year, as usual, the event attracted thousands of people. The head of the Henghe Public Security Bureau, Tu Shaoren, had previously issued a notice prohibiting the event. On the day, he sent patrol officer Lin Cong and eighteen officers to the temple to dissuade the crowd. However, the welcoming crowd not only ignored the warnings but also dragged Lin and the others into the temple. The head of the temple fair ordered the officers to be disarmed, stripped of their uniforms, and have their insignia removed. Their hands were tied behind their backs, and they were hung from the ceiling. They were whipped with leather whips until they fainted, then lowered, and then whipped again. This was repeated four times, leaving them on the verge of death. The other officers were also severely beaten with leather whips, suffering great pain. A peddler secretly reported the incident to the Henghe Public Security Bureau. Upon hearing the news, Director Tu, realizing that the police force was too weak, rushed to the city at night to meet with County Magistrate Miao and request instructions. County Magistrate Miao immediately dispatched patrol officer Xu Guoliang with a large contingent of police officers to rescue them. Lin Cong and the others were eventually rescued by the village chief of Tanhe Village, who knelt down and begged the rioters. After being examined for injuries at the court, they went to the Huiai Hospital for treatment. Lin lost two quick-firing guns and many bullets. The police officers sent by the county government had not returned by late evening, and their fate is unknown.

Rice Shop Robbed in Huxi: Dong Demao's Shunji Rice Shop on Erbanqiao in Huxi, Yongshi, owned by Dong Yicheng, has a thriving business. Yesterday (the sixteenth) at 7:00 PM, the apprentices had already closed the front door. While the shop assistants were having dinner, several robbers suddenly arrived. Two of them broke into the shop, cut the telephone line, and pulled out handguns. Dong and the others, realizing that they were being robbed, did not dare to speak up. One robber, holding a handgun, rushed to the accounting room and stole a small tin box containing foreign currency and silver coins, totaling over a hundred yuan. After the robbery, they fled towards Duanxiang Alley in the northwest.

Shop Owner Kidnapped: In Jiaqiao, Beixiang, Zhenhai, Wang Xiaonong, the owner and manager of the Baoxin Foreign Goods Store, and his family also lived in the store. Unexpectedly, around 11:00 PM the night before, twelve kidnappers suddenly arrived, all carrying handguns and box cannons. They kidnapped the shop owner, Wang Xiaonong. There were three or four members of the security team living in the area, but they did not dare to resist due to the robbers' ferocity and allowed them to be taken away.

Letters 103

Letter from the Secretariat of the Ministry of Railways 104

Dear Sir/Madam,

In your newspaper's headline news on the 12th of this month, it stated, "Jiaoji Railway Buys Boshan Light Railway for Over One Million Yuan, Valued at Over Three Hundred Thousand Yuan." Furthermore, in your newspaper's headline news on the 14th of this month, it stated, "Jiaoji Railway Buys Boshan Railway," claiming that "The Japanese are preventing the Jiaoji Railway from building a branch line from Boshan to the Coal Mine, and are buying the light railway. It is reported that the purchase price has been agreed upon at 1.6 million yuan. The Ministry of Railways, unaware of the truth, is said to have approved the contract." After investigation, our ministry has not received any documents from the Jiaoji Railway regarding this matter, let alone approved any contract. However, since there are records of this, we specifically telegraphed Chairman Yan of the Jiaoji Railway, who also stated that it was absolutely not true. This proves that the news reported by your newspaper is completely fabricated. We hereby request that your newspaper make a correction.

Secretariat of the Ministry of Railways

March 17th

Education News 105

Citywide Sports Meet Closed Yesterday

Athletes' Competitions Completed:: Excellent Results

Will Go to the National Games:: To Showcase Skills

Awards Ceremony Tomorrow Afternoon:: At the Chamber of Commerce

The Shanghai Citywide Sports Meet, which had been rumored for some time, began on the 13th and closed yesterday. Over the past six days, all the results have been very satisfactory. The purpose of this meet was twofold: (1) to bring together various sports competitions in Shanghai to promote teamwork; (2) to select representatives to attend the National Games. It was a unprecedented grand event. The competition committee, in view of the fact that Chinese sports have no rules for amateur and professional athletes, disqualified all athletes suspected of being professional, and did not allow them to participate. In total, three or four male and female athletes who registered to participate or were disqualified after participating were disqualified. This is truly a new era for Chinese sports and good news for the Chinese sports world. The members of the competition committee, disregarding personal feelings, served the public. This spirit is commendable, and the impact will be felt nationwide, which will help revitalize the Chinese sports scene.

Yesterday was the last day of the meet. The events included soccer and men's and women's tennis doubles championships. Newcomers to the tennis world, Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang, defeated Li Huitang and Liu Tieliang yesterday with scores of 6-2, 6-4, and 6-1 to win the men's doubles championship. In women's tennis doubles, Kuai Shuping and Li Yun played against Su Zuqi and Wang Dale, with scores of 3-6, 6-3, and 5-2 (Kuai and Li were ahead). Due to the late hour, the game could not be finished. The details of yesterday are described below.

Soccer Final: Huale Loses, Jinan Wins Championship 106

Result: 3-0

The soccer final between Jinan and Huale took place at the China Baseball Field yesterday afternoon at 3:30 PM. Over two thousand spectators attended, making it a very popular event. From beginning to end, Jinan adopted an enveloping and pressing tactic. Huale's defense was solid, and they managed to keep the score level in the first half. In the second half, after Zhou Xianyan and Li Ning withdrew, the defense was weakened, and Jinan scored three goals in a row, making the score 3-0. Jinan won the championship. Referee Li Silian's record of the match is summarized below.

Military Band Provides Entertainment 107

During the match, the military band invited by the organizers played intermittently in the west stand. The sound was sonorous, adding a lot of interest and opening the minds of the audience.

(2) Appearing on the Silver Screen 108

At 3:15, the two teams lined up on the field and had a film taken. The action during the match was also captured on camera for future commemoration. This film will be shown at the awards ceremony tomorrow, and the appearance of the athletes on the silver screen will surely cause a burst of warm applause.

(3) Cheering Squad Displays Power 109

All of Jinan's students came to the stadium yesterday and gathered in the east stand to carry out their cheering duties. They shouted encouragement during attacks, and the applause was thunderous when they scored. The three cheers at the start of the game were especially majestic. The Huale supporters were also numerous, and the sounds echoed in the air, creating a spirited atmosphere.

(4) Impenetrable Goal 110

Jinan kicked off first and immediately took offensive measures. Huale responded calmly. For the first ten minutes, the momentum was similar, and both sides had opportunities to shoot. After that, the situation became slightly calmer. Then, Jinan became imposing and powerful, and Huale's goal became the target of all attacks, but Zhou Xianyan's skillful operation ensured that there were no mistakes. Jinan attacked again and again, unable to find a way to score. There were two clear chances to score, but they missed them, which was a pity. At the end of the first half, the score was Jinan 0, Huale 0.

(5) Iron Army Scores Three Times 111

The change of sides reduced the excitement, as Li Huitang and Sun Sijing of Huale were less forceful, and the two generals Zhou Xianyan and Li Ning withdrew from the game. The momentum of the game plummeted, and Jinan attacked at will. Huale was initially penalized for a foul, and Dai Linjing scored from a penalty kick, opening the scoring. Shortly after, Tong Rongwen and Dai Linjing scored again, resulting in a 3-0 score and winning the championship.

Men's Tennis Doubles 112

Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang Win Championship

The men's tennis doubles semi-finals were held yesterday afternoon at 10:00 AM. After a short break, the finals were held. As a result, Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang defeated Li Huitang and Liu Tieliang 3-0 to win the championship. The scores were 6-3, 6-4, and 6-1.

Semi-finals: There were two groups. In the first group, Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang were up against Li Zuxun and Guo Jingwu. However, Li and Guo withdrew, so Zheng and Yu won the right to the finals without effort. In the second group, Li Huitang and Liu Tieliang played against Liang Yong and Kuang Yiyun. As a result, Li and Liu won the right to the finals with scores of 6-2, 6-1, and 6-2.

Finals: Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang and Li Huitang and Liu Tieliang, who won the right to the finals, rested for ten minutes and then began to compete. Zheng and Yu were young and handsome, and their tennis skills were extraordinary. Although Li and Liu were veterans, they were not their opponents. However, they were unwilling to show weakness and worked hard to fight. The first set was 6-3, and the second set was 6-4. Victory belonged to Zheng and Yu. From this score, it can be seen that the situation was still fairly balanced. In the third set, the pair of young men launched an even more fierce attack, and Li and Liu found it difficult to defend and were defeated. Zheng and Yu won again 6-1 and won the championship.

Women's Tennis Doubles: Kuai Shuping and Li Lian Win Against Su Zuqi and Wang Dale 113

3-6:: 6-3:: 5-2

Due to the Late Hour, the Game Could Not Be Finished. All Four Players Have Outstanding Skills and Will Be Sent to the National Games

The women's tennis doubles final was held yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM. The contestants were Kuai Shuping and Li Lian against Su Zuqi and Wang Dale. All four players had good skills and performed well, but the game could not be finished due to the late hour. In the first set, Su and Wang won 6-3. In the second set, Kuai and Li won 6-3. In the third set, the score was 5-2 (Kuai and Li were ahead) when it became too dark to continue playing. However, the competition will not continue today either. The committee, in view of the excellent skills of the four players, has decided that they will all represent Shanghai at the National Games. The situation of yesterday's match is described below.

Evaluating the Tennis Skills: All four players have their own strengths. Relatively speaking, Kuai Shuping should be ranked first. Her shots and serves are fast and measured. Su Zuqi's defense is invaluable, and her serves are also very fast. Wang Dale is also not weak, but lacks a bit of grip. Ms. Li Lian is the most stable, making very few mistakes. The backhand shots of Ms. Kuai and Ms. Li are more stable. In short, the performances of all four were excellent and won the praise of the audience.

First Set: The first set started with Kuai serving first, winning a game. Then, Su and Wang's offense was very strong, winning three games in a row, taking the lead with 2-1. However, Kuai and Li did not show weakness, attacking fiercely and Ms. Li feinting to the east and attacking to the west, never missing. Ms. Kuai used powerful shots, making many achievements. Su and Wang suddenly seemed unable to withstand it, creating a score of 3-3. Then, the competition became more intense. The next game was fought for a long time, with repeated ties, making it difficult to judge the winner. Suddenly, Su's net play and Wang's shots were very accurate and fast, winning the game. Su and Wang's momentum increased and they went straight to the top, winning the first set 6-3.

Baseball Championship - Jiaotong University

Swimming Championship - Yu Binqi

Second Set: After losing the first set, Ms. Kuai and Ms. Li worked hard to retaliate and were indeed successful, winning two games in a row. However, after their victory, Su and Wang were unwilling to fall behind and tried hard to catch up, winning two games as well. Then, Kuai and Li won another game, and Su and Wang tied again, making the score 3-3. Kuai and Li were determined to win and worked together to attack. Kuai's strength and Li's soft ball, suddenly left and suddenly right, refused to let go. Su and Wang were so tired of defending that they collapsed, and Kuai and Li also won back the second set with a score of 6-3.

Third Set: With each side having won one set, the outcome was undecided. The decisive battle of the third set was inevitable. Su and Wang had a bad start, and their hand balls could not be returned, so they lost many points. Their opponents took the opportunity to attack and won three games in a row. Although Su and Wang were able to win back a game, Kuai and Li's momentum was strong, and they added to the dimming twilight, successfully winning another game, making the score 5-2. At this time, it was already dark and the lights of thousands of homes were on. The competition was terminated.

Far Eastern Games 116

Venues Have Been Determined

(Tokyo, Japan Press Agency, 18th) The Far Eastern Games Organizing Committee held a meeting at the office of the Sports Promotion Association yesterday at 6:00 PM. Minister Noguchi and 18 committee members attended. They discussed specific arrangements for the venue layout and various other issues. As a result, it was decided to renovate the track and field and soccer venues and to build new goals for the soccer field and floors and lights for the basketball court to facilitate evening games. The design for the swimming pool is scheduled to be completed on the 20th and the work can be completed before the opening of the games. The tennis court problem, which has not been resolved until now, has also been decided to build a new tennis court and spectator stand within the Japan Tennis Association in 5-Nencho Street for the use of the games.

The Fourth Day of the Jiangsu Provincial Games 123

Yesterday, the Public Pre-selection Began. Today and Tomorrow, the Competition Will Continue

The Jiangsu Public Pre-selection Games officially opened yesterday. At 9:30 AM, the opening ceremony was held amidst military music. Attendees included Chu Minyi, Yang Xingfo, Chen Hexian, Yu Qingtang, and hundreds of referees and male and female athletes. The event was a grand spectacle. The situation at the venue and the various results are recorded below.

Venue Order 124

Yesterday, the venue order was maintained by Gao Yunpeng, the director of the discipline department, who invited 90 Zhenjiang Boy Scouts to maintain order throughout the venue. It was extremely solemn. The eight disciplinarians were all students from the police academy, and they worked conscientiously and impartially, adding a lot of color to the event.

Opening Situation 125

At 9:00 AM yesterday, the first day of the Jiangsu Provincial Games for the Public Pre-selection began. First, the commander's platform issued an order to gather all the athletes in the venue. After the ceremony,

Director Yu reported that this Public Games had the participation of more than 30 counties from all over Jiangsu Province. Those in school sacrificed their studies, and those who were employed sacrificed their jobs. They participated with great excitement, making it the first time that Jiangsu had such a large scale athletic meet. Due to time constraints, the facilities were incomplete, but thanks to the enthusiasm of the gentlemen who came to the meeting, we were able to fulfill our obligations and guide everything. Mr. Yang Xingfo originally planned to leave the province today, but was retained by this meeting and is still attending today. Mr. Chu Minyi enthusiastically solicited prizes, up to more than a hundred pieces. Today, Mr. Yang took the night train from Shanghai to Zhen and personally brought a special large silver cup donated by the Shanghai business community, which is particularly touching. There are a total of 525 participants in this session, including 315 men and 44 women in track and field, and 9 soccer teams. I hope that you will work hard to participate with the four major spirits of sportsmanship, cooperation, sacrifice.

Chu Minyi gave a speech on the two meanings of sports: method and purpose. The methods are different for each item, but the purpose is the same: health. There is a health competition in this session, which has not been seen before. Let me explain it. Although our physical education can be measured by sports competition results, it is slightly different from health tests. What we call health competition has three aspects: (1) physical examination (2) physical strength test (3) physical fitness test. It can be called the three tests of health. What is a physical examination? It is to check height, width, weight, etc., just like the height and tonnage of a car. What is a physical strength test? It is to test each person's grip, thrust, pull, etc. It's like using a scale to weigh them. The test table will show the number, which is different from lifting stone burdens and stone locks in the past. If a stone burden is 60 jin, and this person has 70 jin of strength, then of course he has more than enough strength. If this person's strength is tested to be 30 jin, then the 60 jin of stone will naturally not be moved, and there will be no harm. Only if someone has 57 jin of strength, they try to lift 60 jin of stone, and they seem to be struggling halfway, but because of the sake of the face, they are unwilling to show weakness in front of everyone, so they reluctantly lift it up. These extra three jin of exertion are enough to cause injury, which is very dangerous. Therefore, the physical strength test is also like a car with several cylinders and how much horsepower. Overloading can easily damage the car. The fine blood vessels of the human body are very fragile. If you use too much force, they are easily ruptured, which can lead to hemoptysis. The strength test has no such danger. What is a physical fitness test? Suppose A has the same physical condition and strength as B, but the durability of work or the changes after work are different. This is the evidence of different physical fitness. For example, if five people exercise and run at the same time, their pulse, breathing, and temperature should be tested before departure. After the exercise is over, the test is repeated. If a person with lung disease has a higher temperature and pulse, etc., it will immediately increase. If the person has not returned to normal after ten minutes, then it can be seen that the person is not healthy. Therefore, increasing a person's physical fitness is to increase the life resistance. It is like a car with the same height, width, and horsepower, but its ability to travel a certain number of miles without breaking down depends on how much endurance it has. The above three points are the elements of a health competition. Gentlemen, you are here today, some from schools and some from professional institutions. Since elementary school, you have been exercising to develop the ability to serve. The various sports activities should be gradually created on weekdays, and you cannot embrace the Buddha's feet on the spur of the moment. Those who are employed have been out of school for a long time and do not seem to like sports very much, but if they can not forget the school's sports, they can increase their service durability and productivity will definitely increase accordingly. Therefore, health has a direct relationship with the national economy. If you are healthy individually, your children will be healthy. Extending from the individual to the country, the health of the nation is also the responsibility of the gentlemen present.

Health Competition 138

Staff and Guest Relay Race, Guard Team Martial Arts Performance

The health competition, initiated by Mr. Chu Minyi, uses a 100-meter race among individuals of the same age group to test their pulse and respiratory rate before starting as the standard. The increase or decrease in these rates at the finish line, compared to the starting point, is used to assess their physical fitness. Mr. Chu first invited Yang Xingfo, Chen Hexian, Yu Qingtang, Jiang Shunyuan, and Sun Daosheng, a reporter from this newspaper, to demonstrate the process. Subsequently, participants included Ms. Tao Xuan, a member of the Central Legislative Yuan, Mrs. Chen Hexian, women's champion Hu Ruisheng, and over forty other female participants. The results of each participant will be reviewed by Mr. Chu and Mr. Yang before a final decision is made.

Yesterday, over thirty members of the provincial government guard team gave a temporary performance of various martial arts and calisthenics, which was quite spectacular. As the competition neared its end, Yang Xingfo, Yu Qingtang, and other presenting guests participated in a 400-meter relay race. Important staff, newspaper reporters, and female school instructors, sixteen people in total, joined, divided into four groups. When the starting gun fired, participants bravely and fiercely competed. The intense competition resembled that of the games' athletes. Thunderous applause accompanied them along the way. The winning group was composed of Chen Hexian, Zheng Xigu, Sun Daosheng, and Pei Shunyuan, with a time of 1 minute 5.8 seconds.

News 148

Actively Preparing for the National Education Conference

With the National Education Conference on April 15th approaching, the documentation section of the preparatory committee held a meeting at 3 PM on the 17th in the Ministry of Education conference room. Hosts Zhao Shu, Zhou Buyu, and other clerks of the documentation section discussed the following matters in general: (A) Distribution of work: (1) Conference recording divided into shorthand and clerical. Four clerks, two shorthand reporters. (2) Receipt and dispatch of documents. (3) Storage of documents. (4) Processing of documents. For each of the above items, except for the shorthand reporters (two people), where there were concerns about the number of people being insufficient and where allocation was slightly delayed, the rest were distributed. (B) Allocation of daily office rotation duties before the meeting. (C) Recent matters to be handled (such as statistics on registered personnel; notifying the reception section as people successively register, in order to prepare reception, etc.). It is also heard that from the 18th onwards, the preparatory committee will begin working at the Ministry of Education Club location (fortunately, most of the preparatory staff are Ministry of Education employees. Apart from urgent and important ad hoc meetings, they usually come to the club around 3 PM in the afternoon for rotating office duties). All preparatory matters related to the national education conference prior to this, such as receiving and dispatching documents, etc., which were handled concurrently by the general affairs division, will be accepted and handled by the preparatory committee from the 18th onwards until the meeting site. It is heard that Central University’s buildings are currently insufficient for its own use and is negotiating to borrow the Ministry of Railways auditorium, which is largely settled. It is said that a lease has been negotiated for the third floor of the Central Hotel to be the lodging place for the conference members.

The 16th Standing Committee meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Public Secondary School Joint Association was held on the 13th at Zhenjiang Middle School. Xue Liangshu was publicly elected chairman, and Hu Aigu served as recorder. The ceremony was performed as usual.

Chairman's Report: A total of 23 schools are present today. The school proposals include five from Xizhong, five from Taicang Middle School, six from Shangzhong, three from Zhenzhong, four from this association, and other ad hoc proposals.

Matters for Discussion 1. Whether to amend the constitution of this association. Resolved: Please have the standing committee members amend the constitution of this association and then submit it for discussion. 2.
