Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 230

— Sea Traveler

Husband——Your father is so annoying. Since I married you, it has been a year. Every time I go to see him during this year, he always asks me for money.

Wife——You have to forgive him. He's in the car business. They have an installment plan. When a customer buys a car, they can pay in installments. You married me, like buying a car. You give him money, and that's paying in installments.

Doctor——In any case, you must rest well and avoid crowded and noisy places.

Patient——Oh, doctor. Doing that would really hinder my profession, because I am a pickpocket.

Female music student——Sir, why don't you praise my voice? All my neighbors say I can go abroad to study.

Music Professor——Only because I don't live next door to you.

A——Don't be so disappointed. As long as the green hills remain, there will always be firewood to burn. As long as a person lives in the world, there will always be a day to be proud.

B——But I don't think so. Because my family runs a coffin shop. If I want to be proud, the more people die, the better.

Politician——Today I have a cold and a hoarse throat and can't speak.

Secretary——But you must speak. I have already sent your speech to the newspapers.

Overseas Tea Talk 231

— Tian Peng, from Tokyo

Door Ticket for Waste Utilization The famous musician, Ms. Anna, recently held a concert in Moscow. Her admission tickets were unique, using old items instead of gold coins, and costing six pounds of rags, waste paper, lead cans, fish bones, and old boots. Those who heard about it couldn't help but smile. In fact, the government intends to collect waste for utilization to enrich the national treasury.

Lament of the English Pastor The senior students of Oxford University have recently become popular with wearing red and blue clothing, imitating the American movie star Ronald Lo, and competing to grow beards. This American-style craze will spread everywhere. The stubborn pastors in English capital are all lamenting, saying that it is a great worry for the world and the human heart.

Resolution of the Barber Conference The Austrian city of Wei recently held a barbers' conference. The chairman said that the popularity of safe self-use knives in recent years has deprived us of a part of our business. It is our great enemy and we should seek ways to resist it. It was resolved to persuade customers not to keep William-style mustaches and to shave completely so that they can grow easily and our business can recover.

New outfit for women's bathrobes Women's bathrobes have always used tight-fitting suits. When worn, the hidden places are vaguely visible, and after bathing, the water sticks to the flesh, making the lower body more realistic, which is not elegant. Since last year, clothing stores in various countries have tied a wide cloth hanging from the chest. It is expected to become popular soon.

Results of the Hell Exam After the semester exams in the capital of Hungary's primary schools, the results were posted and sent to the families of each student. On that day, more than 100 students from Jin'cheng Primary School suddenly disappeared. The police and parents were panicked. It was said that the exams had become hell. The East and the West are in the same situation. Japanese people have even committed suicide because of failing the exam.

Anecdotes of the Indian Bathing Festival 232

— Dai Xiaozhong

Since the National People's Party leader Gandhi in India actively implemented a non-violent resistance policy to seek independence and freedom for the Indian people, the world has been shocked and the great powers have been watching, attracting much attention. Recently, the bathing festival was held in SANGAME, a holy place in India. Everyone left their lanes, and the whole country went crazy. The number of participants was about 3.5 million. The enthusiasm of the Indian people for religion is evident. The bathing festival is bizarre and colorful. The Times recently reported it in detail, which is quite interesting. I have translated a few excerpts for readers to discuss.

Barbers Prosper Tenfold. A single hair is but a drop in the ocean, yet the Indian people regard it as precious as a jade disc. It is said that if a person donates a hair and throws it into the Ganges River, he can be spared ten thousand reincarnations. Young widows believe this even more firmly. When the time comes, they entrust their three thousand strands of sorrow to a single cut, without hesitation. As a result, three thousand barbers are overwhelmed and unable to cope. In an instant, countless believers are as bare as Niu Mountain after being濯濯 (deforested).

Seeking Heavenly Blessings Leads to Ruin and Destitution. When tens of thousands of people worship and pray, and the heat of their devotion reaches the boiling point, some believers donate their belongings to priests in exchange for intangible happiness. Afterwards, they do not hesitate to turn to charitable organizations or the local police for help. Their foolish sincerity is unmatched. Local officials find it particularly difficult to deal with these believers.

Treading on Burning Fire: A Grand Self-Sacrificing Performance. The most amazing and breathtaking performance during the bathing festival is undoubtedly the fire-walking performance. All believers who are well-versed in this practice take this opportunity to show off their skills. First, they tie their feet to a three-legged frame, hang upside down, their heads only a foot away from the ground. A large pile of burning fuel is placed on the ground, and the flames are raging, but the performer's expression is normal, as if not feeling the slightest pain. However, this is not enough to be surprising. One SWANMI is able to walk barefoot on a pile of burning coal with thousand-foot flames, as if walking on flat ground, talking and laughing freely, and taking it as a pleasure. It is truly a spectacle.

Leftover Elegies 233

— Tao An

Elegiac couplets, although a minor skill, require ingenuity and clever ideas. The books contain many fine works that are not mundane or afflicted with obscure allusions. Works that are both outstanding and free from these faults are rare. I happened to visit Mr. Cheng Lenglin at 蠖廬 and had a long conversation with him about ancient and modern times to relieve my loneliness. Then, we touched on the art of couplets. He told me two elegiac couplets, whose author I do not know. The sentences are simple, and the meaning is elegant. I recorded the actual conversation to share with readers. The couplets are:

"Eighty-two years, muddled and confused, a scholar or a doctor? The flowing water is merciless, let it go.

September 1st, clear and distinct, the dream is over, the drunkenness is over, pick a flower and smile, wait for me to return."

"(One)

"The fate of husband and wife, unfinished in this life, will be completed in the next.

The debt of children, borrowed by two, repaid by one." (Two).

Interesting Anecdotes of Painting 234

— Zheng Yimei

Recently, many painters have vowed to paint Buddha images. Qian Binghe of Wuxing is one of them. Binghe's Buddha images have different appearances, washing away the disease of dullness. One day, he painted a Buddha sitting under a bodhi tree. After completion, he hung it up and stared at it, and suddenly laughed. It turned out that it looked exactly like the comedian Xu Zhuodai. Knowing that I often associate with Zhuobao, he immediately inscribed it and entrusted it to a mounting shop, asking me to give it to him. The inscription is quite readable, saying: "Thirty years in Shanghai, suddenly opened up a different idea. Preaching with a brush, regretting the past. Floating and sinking in politics, disturbing people's affairs. Karma cycles, quicker than shadows. Nowhere to avoid Qin, the fisherman sighs in vain. Sitting quietly in meditation, away from the dust. Playfully imitating the respected face, mounting it into a Buddha image. A celebrity incarnated, the abbot of an ancient temple. Dense forest, deep mountain, plump body, broad mind. Not worth a smile, just for pure appreciation."

In his later years, Wu Changshuo enjoyed great fame. Even people from Japan were honored to obtain his works. However, when Wu was living in Wuxia, he was impoverished. At the end of the year, he could not even afford a dou of wine and a chicken to comfort himself. So, he painted a four-foot-long painting, with one fish, one chicken, one pig's trotter, and one jar of wine. After finishing the painting, he added a playful inscription and asked his servant to take it to the market to sell it. He got three gold coins, which were enough to buy chicken, fish, pig's trotter, and a jar of wine. This was because prices were lower at that time, unlike today. Wu Changshuo was drunk and slept soundly until New Year's Day, when he woke up to the sound of firecrackers ringing in the new year. Wu Changshuo considered it the only happy thing in his life and often mentioned it when talking with friends.

Travel Notes of Southeast Asia (11) 235

— Linghua

Along the way, there are signs that say "Taoist Temple", but they are actually opium dens. Is there any Tao in this? The name is elegant. Some people run public opium dens, some are rickshaw pullers, buying rickshaws and renting them to locals and collecting taxes, and some are brothels. There is a large shed labeled "Chinese Men and Women Technical Troupe." There are various small vendors, such as those selling bamboo 地牟 cows near the Guangzhou Bund. When released, they make a營營 sound, and children gather to watch. There are many musical instruments in the store. I hope someone will advocate for a national music association to influence society through art. There are also Jingwu Athletic Association and other sports associations. If society can be transformed through sports, art, and music, the effect will be great. There are many pharmacies selling plasters, pills, powders, and ginseng, as well as small fortune-telling shops for men and women. Some are called female Taoist fortune-tellers. Superstition is universal, both in the East and the West. In the Xujiahui Catholic Church in Shanghai, there are many bronze and clay sculptures and colorful paintings of heaven and hell, all variations of Buddhist monks. In the Sensoji Temple in Asakusa, Japan, there are dozens of fortune-tellers, especially female ones. But France and Japan are not harmed in their prosperity. Now, there are many conflicts in our country because of this. It is important to implement things in an orderly manner.

People here have breakfast at 11 am, take a nap at 12 pm, and get up after 2 pm. But it is difficult to say for laborers. In the afternoon, I visited the product exhibition hall of the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, which is quite impressive. This is the center of the overseas Chinese.

Most overseas Chinese families worship Guan Gong. This originated with Shanxi merchants. Shanxi merchants are everywhere, and there are Guan Gong temples everywhere, which are also chambers of commerce. Guan Gong was from 解州, Shanxi. Because of his loyalty and righteousness, he is admired by the people of Shanxi. This spread throughout the country through merchants. The reason why merchants especially worship him is because Liu Bei, Guan Yu, and Zhang Fei became sworn brothers, sharing interests and life and death without wavering, which is a good model for forming partnerships to start businesses in distant lands. They gather at Guan Gong temples every year to calculate accounts and to warn people's conscience. The overseas Chinese have adopted this and promoted its spirit globally, forming a Guan Gong religion. Everything arises from need, and it is not accidental. Also, those overseas are lonely without organizations, making it difficult to survive. To form an organization, a name must be chosen. The righteousness of Taoyuan is a good model for sworn brotherhood and a successful organization that should not be criticized. Our people have not been able to acquire the knowledge of Greek and Roman colonial culture, the strength of the Hanseatic League in the Middle Ages, or the scientific organization of modern European autonomous colonial cooperation. They only trace back to a method of heteronymous combination of ethnic groups as a symbol of collective life for outward development. It is also pitiful.

European Correspondence (45) 236

— Liu Haisu

Andre Derain (1)

Two days after returning to Paris from Switzerland, Zhang Xian and Wu Hengqin brought me four or five newspapers. When I opened them, they all reported on the exhibition of masterpieces by Renoir, Cézanne, Matisse, Derain, and Modigliani at the BEUJEUIMJEIUNE Gallery at 83 RUE DU FAUBOURG. To be honest, these names were not new to me. I had seen their works in Japan before, but they were not their best works. However, I had long sympathized with Renoir's trembling flesh, Cézanne's color scales, and Matisse's savage decorative tastes.

The next afternoon, we took a motorcycle from HOTEL DES FACULTES to the BEUJEUJMUENE Gallery at 83 RUE DES FAUBOURG. These galleries are not art museums, but art dealers' shops. This number 83 is the largest and most famous art shop in Paris. The owner, BEUJENUIJMEUNE, used to specialize in collecting works by Impressionist masters before they became famous. Later, he made a fortune. Even now, his collection is considered the richest. So, I often go there to see paintings. There were many people inside that day. I walked in and saw Renoir's nude paintings hanging on the left wall of the first room in the center. There were twelve small ones. Next to them were his still life paintings. Further in, a Cézanne "Bathers" was hanging in the middle of the opposite wall, flanked by two "Still Lifes" and "Portrait of Madame Cézanne". I had seen these masterpieces in photographs and bought colored prints. I never thought that the originals would be here. It really aroused my interest. I stood there and looked at them for a long time. I felt that the tight effect of the colors interacting with each other was very different from the prints. The charm of the original was even more unexpected. Further on were eight figures and still life paintings by Matisse. The beautiful and bright colors were as stimulating as seeing the bright scenery in Southeast Asia. He was truly able to obtain the decorative function of color. On the right wall were Derain's works. In this room, he had fourteen large works. In the middle hung a figure painting as large as a one hundred. It was his most famous masterpiece, "The Singer" ARLEQUIN ET PIERROT. To the left was a large painting "Reclining Nude". To the right was his "Greek Woman" FEMME GRECQUE painted in 1919. The remaining two landscapes, one "Flower", and six "Portraits". This is really the most noteworthy of many famous paintings. After seeing them, I gradually walked further inside. In the middle was another large "Still Life" by Derain, depicting many kitchen utensils. Next to it was a large loaf of bread. There were many sketches of him on both sides of the painting. Next to it was Matisse's painting. The paintings of these masters were displayed competitively relative to each other. Presumably, because they all had a common painting style and were also giants of special creation, putting them together could make people recognize several ancestors of the new era. Among them, Matisse and Derain, who are still alive, especially hold the hegemony of the modern European art system. There are so many famous paintings here, but the most eye-catching are still several of Derain's largest paintings. His color scheme is very strong. He draws on Courbet's solidity, Cézanne's sublimity, the black man's simplicity, and the Gothic's melancholy. He has no preconceived plan for painting. What he painted yesterday, he may discard today. Or, if he is interested, he may continue tomorrow. He loves simplicity. He loves things that are innocent. He loves to use black. Even when he uses green, it is very dark. As for the blue, it is often as deep as steel. His white is as white as snow, and he uses a few specks of soot. He uses ochre to depict sensuality. The ups and downs of his paintings are powerful and melodic. When he paints still life, there is no pretense. They are all simple or broken things used in daily life. A wine glass without a foot, or a rice bowl, a string of leftover grapes, a tattered tablecloth are often seen on his paintings. He wants to evoke an emotion from things that have been peeled off. This giant is alive now and cherishes his life very much. He must not be bound by anyone, nor is he enslaved by matter. He uses his independent life to directly express the visual of phenomena. He is the only modern artist who can continue the artistic style of the Middle Ages. At the same time, he is full of the spirit of the living modern.

Chinese Medical Association Invites Hoffman to Lecture 242

The Syphilis Problem Today

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Medical Association will hold its second monthly meeting of the year tonight (March 19th) at 8:00 PM at the YMCA on Sichuan Road. Dr. Hoffman, a renowned German medical scientist, has been invited to lecture on "The Syphilis Problem Today." Dr. Hoffman, who co-discovered the "syphilis pathogen" with Professor Schaudinn of Germany in 1905, has conducted extensive research on this issue and is expected to deliver an insightful presentation. In addition to inviting Chinese and foreign medical organizations to attend, the association welcomes local practitioners to participate.

Rush to Import and Export to Avoid Taxes 243

Japanese Ships Arriving Fully Loaded

According to the World News Agency, with the full implementation of the customs gold unit system after March 16th, there has been a surge in tax-avoidance imports. Japanese goods such as sugar, cotton yarn, cloth, paper, and sundry items have seen a significant increase in arrivals since March. For example, the Ikoma, Kasagi, and Rokko ships, which arrived starting on the 2nd, unloaded a total of 9,441 tons in Shanghai, with 827 tons for Yangtze River transit, almost all fully loaded. On average, each ship carried over 5-600 tons of tax-avoidance goods. At the same time, exports to Japan of cotton seeds, powdered materials, rapeseed, etc., are also very substantial.

Pan-European Beauty Pageant Held in Paris 244

Greek Woman Wins First Place

Paris dispatch: A beauty pageant was recently held in Paris to elect the "Miss Europe". Participants came from twenty countries. The winner of the title of "Miss Europe" was Ms. Dibra Laraco from Greece, followed by Ms. Berlise from Belgium and Ms. Lapurce from France, both of whom were considered the most beautiful women in their respective countries. The event was a grand spectacle with beautiful flowers. The first-place winner, Ms. Dibra Laraco, is known for her beauty in Greece. The elected beauties will travel to the United States to compete with American dancers in order to determine the world's most beautiful woman.

Youth Corner

Clara Bow 245

— Yun Zhi

It was a rainy dusk in early spring. The low, drawn-out sound of the Guangdong bun seller in the alley was already harmonizing with the fine, insistent rain to create an "alley symphony." Such irritating weather was simply stifling.

Upstairs in the front building, three young men were engaged in a heated debate with a friend from Jiangwan. M was buried in writing something, interjecting with occasional jokes. L, his face flushed and veins bulging, was waving his fists, arguing loudly and excitedly with S from Jiangwan. C, who had originally sparked the debate, was siding with L's opponent, often supplementing S's arguments. They all seemed to have lost themselves in the discussion.

"No matter how you look at it, Clara Bow represents the decadence of the capitalist era. She has physical beauty, intoxicating eyes, and passionate kisses. She is the sole representative of American civilization today!" S said.

"If Clara Bow can represent modern American civilization, then the evils of capitalism have only produced one Clara Bow, which has nothing to do with anti-capitalism. But why is the world panicking about capitalism? Clara Bow is simply a manifestation of the evils of Hollywood under the control of capital," L retorted.

C, after a short "break," could no longer restrain himself and burst out like an erupting Mount Fuji, "I welcome capitalism! Because the power of capitalism is irresistible. The rapid rotation of machines and the drastic changes in human culture are all results of capitalism. For example, hasn't the JAZZ of New York influenced Shanghai? If there are still people who oppose machines and the JAZZ of the metropolis, they should just follow Yesenin (a Russian poet who committed suicide) and become ghosts!"

M, who had been holding a pen, spoke for the fourth time, "I don't oppose capitalism, and I don't oppose JAZZ, but I oppose Clara Bow. She is not as great as S and C claim. She has physical beauty, can KISS, is boisterous—but can these really represent American civilization? It's still questionable. For example, what has Clara Bow shown in the recently performed TALKYIDANGERARURNURVE? She was more sensual in REDHAIR. At most, she can represent the American woman shaped by capitalism today."

"No, we know that the representatives of the two major trends in modern civilization are Russia and America, and these two civilizations are impacting the entire world. No one can resist. And Clara Bow is precisely the capitalist type of woman. She is undoubtedly the embodiment of American civilization, and Clara Bow exposes everything on her person," C said.

"But, although Clara Bow can represent a part of American women, she is not as great as you admire. She is a natural phenomenon, and your kind of blind faith is inappropriate," L said.

S said, "No, an actor who can use her talent to portray a social model on the stage or screen is certainly great!"

"Of course, an actor with skill who can portray a certain type of society can be considered successful, but she is not great. Because artistic success and greatness are not the power of one person alone, especially in theater and film, which are multifaceted syntheses. If Clara Bow is good at performing, she is merely a worker in an art production workshop. What's the point of worshiping blindly? Besides, whether she is successful is still subject to our careful criticism," M said.

"Heat!" S replied loudly.

"Yes," C interjected, "Heat, heat is the source of modern culture! All machines, JAZZ, must be hot! Heat is what we should worship! Those who don't understand Clara Bow don't deserve to be modern youths!" C was truly agitated.

"Okay, okay!" S clapped his hands and shouted. L was furious. "No talking about Clara Bow! Those who want to talk can get out!"

"We insist on talking! We insist on talking!" S and C said in unison.

"Get out!" L was really angry now.

"Hey, hey, hey!" M threw down his pen and stood up, gesturing with both hands, "Let's stop talking, gentlemen. Don't you feel hungry?"

"Don't talk!" L added again.

"That's right, you're debating Clara Bow here. What if Clara Bow knew?" M said to S and C, "She would give each of you a loud KISS, like in (Curved Love)!" M then turned to L, "At the same time, if Clara Bow came and kissed you in front of you, you wouldn't object, would you?"

Everyone laughed unnaturally.

Outside, the rain was still falling. The delivery man happily brought up a large pot of food. S grabbed an umbrella and ran downstairs. C chased after him, saying as he walked, "Going back to Jiangwan!"

During the meal, only the sounds of bowls and chopsticks could be heard. Clara Bow had been swallowed into their bellies.

Youth Corner Submission Guidelines 246

(1) The text should focus on discussions of youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, etc. The style is not limited.

(2) Drawings should be limited to youth-related issues.

(3) Photographs of youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, dramas, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movement photography are all welcome, regardless of individuals or groups.

(5) The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the paper.

(6) Do not write horizontally, and avoid writing in a careless manner. Western text should be omitted where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it should be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink for drawings, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please indicate that submissions are for the Youth Corner.

(9) Submissions will not be returned whether they are published or not. If you need them returned, you must state this in advance and attach sufficient postage.

(10) Remuneration for articles is divided into three categories: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. The same applies to drawings and photographs per piece. For special submissions, remuneration will be calculated separately.

Automotive News 247

Special Commentary

Grand Opening of the New York International Automobile Exhibition (Part 2) 248

Huang Yingdai

▲ Durant 1930 Model Durant New Car. There are two types of new six-cylinder cars. The most notable aspect of the large six-cylinder car in terms of construction is the adoption of four-speed acceleration, with the gears completely silent when using the third gear. It is equipped with a 3-something x 4-something L-HEAD engine with 70 horsepower. The small six-cylinder also uses the same engine, but slightly smaller than the former, approximately 34-1 x 4-something, with 58 horsepower. The bodies of both of the above-mentioned new cars are newly manufactured, with a beautiful and charming style. According to the company, the new body is not only beautiful, but also longer than the old style.

Erskine 1930 Model Erskine New Car. This is a product of the Studebaker factory. The construction completely adopts a new method. According to the factory, the weight of the new car itself has considerable strength per pound, and is given a special name: Dynamic New Erskine. It also uses a six-cylinder L-HEAD engine with 70 horsepower. The engine's bore and stroke are 34-3 x 43-1 inches. The wheelbase is 114 inches. The body has also been reformed and is pleasing to the eye.

Essex The new Essex car has a powerful six-cylinder engine. Although there is no reform in terms of length, the internal structure is completely different from the old car. The wheelbase has been increased to 113 inches, 2 and 1/2 inches longer than the old car. The body and interior have novel styles, all with special advantages. The roof, heat reduction device, and ladder for entering the car are all newly reformed and very satisfactory.

Graham Paige The 1930 model new cars produced by Graham-Paige Company have slightly changed in name compared to the old models. Among them, the passenger car named Graham is the company's latest product. The new cars include one type of eight-cylinder car, with a starting horsepower of only 10, and a wheelbase of 122 inches. It is also divided into two types: one with three-speed acceleration and one with four-speed. The third gear is completely silent during acceleration. The body structure and style are similar to the old cars, but the latter's equipment is more complete. As for the new six-cylinder cars with three-speed and four-speed acceleration and a wheelbase of 115 inches long, the construction method is completely the same. Other Graham new cars also have two types of four-speed acceleration, with wheelbase lengths of 127 inches and 137 inches respectively. The style of the body is completely new, and the color of the roof, heat reduction device, and ladder is particularly beautiful and spectacular.

Hudson Hudson has a large eight-cylinder new car on display at the exhibition. This new car is better than the factory's large six-cylinder car. The Hudson engine is also an L-HEAD type, with a bore and stroke of 2/43 x 4/21 inches. The horsepower is 80. The wheelbase is divided into two types: one is 115 inches and the other is 126 inches. The body structure completely adopts a new style, beautiful and dazzling, unprecedented. The most satisfying car equipment is the Day Light sedan installed on both Hudson and Essex cars. It can accommodate five people, and the price is extremely low. There are two doors, both equipped with hinged doors. The top can be folded up, completely concealing the glass, transforming it into a factory car.

Hupmobile Hupmobile has a large eight-cylinder new car, which was recently manufactured, with 133 horsepower. In terms of speed, it can travel 90 miles per hour. The engine is an L-HEAD type, with a bore of 3 and 1/2 inches and a stroke of 3 and 3/4 inches. The engine's carburetion system also uses a down-draft type and has a cold water device to monitor overheating. Therefore, even when using the strongest speed, the engine will not experience any accidents, preventing damage to the vehicle and increasing its lifespan. In addition, Hupmobile's new car exhibition also features an eight-cylinder car with 100 horsepower and a six-cylinder car with 70 horsepower, both of which are excellent products.

Lincoln Except for some unimportant parts that have been slightly reformed, the rest of the new Lincoln car is the same as the old car. However, Lincoln's body, with its sophisticated construction and beautiful style, has long been praised by the public. The body of this new car still does not lose its inherent position.

Marmon Marmon has two types of straight-eight-cylinder new cars on display at the exhibition, namely the 869 and 879 models.

The former is priced at US$1,500 and the latter at US$2,000. When these eight-cylinder cars were first manufactured, they were originally priced around US$3,000, while the Roosevelt brand was priced at US$1,000. The interiors of the 869 and 879 new cars are extremely spacious, the power is extremely strong, beyond the reach of existing cars, and the engine's construction is also excellent, equipped with an LBEAD combustion chamber. According to the factory, this combustion chamber can greatly increase the speed of the car.

The car is produced by the Buick factory and is priced at approximately US$1,000. It uses an LBEAD engine with a bore of 3/81 x 4/85 inches, and a horsepower of 67.5. The wheelbase is 110 inches. The internal braking system is also automatic.

Among them, there is one type of eight-cylinder car, using a dual-material power generation system, which is used to replace the old six-cylinder car. The dual-material power generation system of the six-cylinder new car replaces the old special six-cylinder car, while the ordinary six-cylinder new car replaces the standard six-cylinder old car. The car tops and windows of all new cars are larger than the old cars. The eight-cylinder new cars are all equipped with shatterproof glass, using pop-up pistons, and the engine is 3/41 x 4/21 inches. The horsepower is approximately 100. The wheelbase is divided into two types: one is 118 inches long and the other is 128 and 1/4 inches long. Twenty-Four Cylinder Car Ding Zuce

Kay Don, a famous British racing driver, is specially manufacturing a great car named Silver Bullet in order to win the 1930 world speed record. This competition is imminent and will still be held at the Daytona Beach racetrack in Florida, USA.

The Silver Bullet racing car is long and narrow like a whale. The state is shown in the attached picture. In the picture, half of the outer shell has been removed, and the internal machinery is completely exposed. A is the ice-cooled radiator, B and C are two continuous engines, each with twelve cylinders, manufactured by the British Sunbeam Motor Car Company. D is the supercharger, E is the carburetor, E is the steering gear, G is the exhaust pipe, H is the rudder tail, J is the water pump, K is the connecting crankshaft, L is the intake pipe, M is the clutch, M is the drive shaft, and is the gearbox.

The car is 30 feet long and 44 inches wide. The length seems amazing, but because its width and height are very small, at first glance almost no one knows the greatness of its internal mechanical power.

Both the front and rear axles are suspended under semi-elliptical springs. Although the form of the springs is similar to that of ordinary cars, the steel sheets are unusually wide and the distance between the upper and lower springs is only one inch at most. This is because it is intended to prevent the wheels from being skewed during high-speed driving.

The engine is two twelve-cylinder engines connected in a straight line. Each engine has six cylinders on each side, forming a V shape. Each cylinder has four valves, located in four corners on the cylinder head. There are two exhaust valves and two intake valves. In the center of the four valves is the spark plug. The eccentric camshaft that opens and closes the valves is located on the top of the cylinder and transmits power from the front end of the engine to operate it. Each bearing on the crankshaft uses steel column bearings, so it can rotate up to 4,000 revolutions per minute. Each engine weighs about 1,000 pounds and can generate 2,000 horsepower. It is estimated that each half pound of the machine body generates one horsepower, which is the greatest new contribution to the engineering world.

Nowadays, high-speed engines all use superchargers to

increase their horsepower. The Silver Bullet is no exception, and the supercharger installed is quite large. It is a large-diameter centrifugal type that draws in oil and gas from two carburetors and blows it into the cylinders at high pressure. Although the two engines are connected as one, their crankshafts are not directly connected in a straight line. Instead, another shaft is set up under these two crankshafts, using gears to transmit power to the lower shaft. The speed of the lower shaft is twice as fast as the crankshaft. It is said that this structure can avoid the torsional force directly applied to the crankshaft when entering.

The Silver Bullet car is prepared to travel at a high speed of 200 to 300 miles per hour. At such a high speed, its brakes must be very safe to avoid danger. Therefore, the construction of the brakes is extremely novel. Each brake wheel is made by cutting a steel block weighing about 400

pounds into a copper bowl weighing 45 pounds. This alone shows the prudence in its manufacture. The application of the brakes is driven by liquid pressure, and to prevent it from generating high heat, a water cooling device is installed.

In order to avoid wind resistance, the shape of the car body uses a streamline everywhere. Not only that, the bottom of the car body is completely sealed, covering all the internal mechanical parts. This is in case it rushes into the sea (note that the American racing driver Lockhart was once swept into the sea by waves last year, and then hit back to the beach by the waves, so it can still be used to float). In front of the driver's seat, a thick nickel-steel screen is used to prevent the engine from catching fire and to prevent the driver from being crushed in the event of a collision.

The structure of all parts of the car can be said to encompass everything that humans can think of, such as the use of the tail rudder to prevent the forward skew, and the position of the fuel tank behind the driver's seat, making it completely avoid the heat of the engine compartment. It is impossible to list them all.

According to the world record of car speed, it has been increasing year by year. In the most recent three years, the winners of the championship have all been British. In 1928, it was created by Campbell of England. Its speed was 214.797 miles. The racing car was named Bluebird, with 1,000 horsepower. In 1929, it belonged to Segrave of England. The speed reached 231.36 miles. The racing car was named Golden Arrow, also with 1,000 horsepower. This year's Silver Bullet racing car has 4,000 horsepower, and its performance must be impressive.

Scientific Perspective on Automobile Business by Cheng Zhizheng 251

Failures Can Be Easily Improved After Analyzing Twelve Points

Modern times are a scientific world. Everything, everything, tends to be scientific, and doing business is also aimed at scientific methods. The so-called scientific method has a very broad meaning, but to summarize and generalize it, the scientific method is to do things in an orderly manner and to be able to analyze. In business, analysis is especially important. In meritorious times, we must study how to succeed, and in times of failure, we must study how to fail. Find the cause of the failure, and then study it and improve it. The business will naturally flourish. But to say that the automobile business occupies a great and superior position in modern industry and commerce, its management and management must be able to use scientific methods. Recently, the Automotive Weekly published twelve reasons for the failure of the automobile business, and the analysis is extremely clear, which can help the general automobile business. Therefore, I translated this article.

(1) The business work does not work hard to observe the problem of employment using scientific methods. The first is to study efficiency. Therefore, the efficiency of working for one minute is greater than the value of working for a quarter of an hour without efficiency. If the automobile company does not pay attention to this level and does not find ways to improve efficiency, failure is undoubtedly. Therefore, whenever it is seen that the staff is not working hard, methods should be taken to improve it. The improvement methods are also very resolute, such as bonus fees, stock sharing system, etc. How to use it will not be discussed in this article for the time being.

(2) The machine is not good Some automobile companies buy old machines for cheap. As a result, the quality of the goods produced is too poor, and the service performance is too poor. The business will inevitably gradually dim down. Some companies buy new machines, but they are not good at choosing, or they only choose cheap ones, so the same result will occur.

(3) Intellectual advertising In the automobile business, what cannot be saved the most is an advertising fee. However, the same advertisement is published, and the effect received by Company A and Company B is different. Maybe Company A spent more money, but the effect is not as good as Company B. Therefore, advertisements cannot be published casually. We must study which newspapers and magazines have the largest sales volume and which advertisements are the most eye-catching and can get the greatest effect, but cost the most economical money. This point seems very small, but the key to the success or failure of the company is completely tied to it. The losses of many companies are the result of poor advertising.

(4) Not good at selecting business during operation There are many automobile service companies in various parts of the United States. The businesses they operate are naturally different. Or washing cars or lubricating cars. Before opening, they should choose the specialties. Do not choose more poor people, because if there is too much work, the clues will be complicated. The work is not specialized, and the command is difficult to be satisfactory. The efficiency is extremely low. Therefore, the selection of business must be extremely careful.

(5) Insufficient or too much capital Capital depends on the scope of business. If the scope is wide, if the capital is less, it will not be able to turn around. If the scope is small, if the capital is large, it will only lose money. Those who are good at business are most sensitive to this. When to increase capital and when to reduce it can all meet its needs without wasting it. Moreover, it is necessary to plan for the financial market in advance, so as not to dig wells when thirsty, and capital has to borrow with huge interest. This kind of early understanding is of course in everyone's mind. 

(6) Making unnecessary competition Unnecessary competition is also the main cause of failure. The so-called "cut-throat competition" (CNTTBROATCOWPETITION) is both harmful and unprofitable, and must not exist. Even if there are many peers in one place, the prices should be unified and agreed upon. This is the right way. Moreover, it is not necessarily welcome for customers to win customers' hearts with low prices, because they only hope for good service. The price is higher, as long as the service is good, they do not ask. On the contrary, if the price is too low, they will definitely suspect the poor service and the goods are not refined.

(7) No credit standards It is very common to do business and pay on account, but we must also pay attention to the credit standard of this person. If he has no credit, and you put out a huge amount of money, the result will be that the money cannot be recovered, and your own capital will be greatly affected. Making a cocoon and binding yourself will burn you to death. Why bother?

(8) Too much small business What is small business? That is, most of the customers are small businesses, but there are very few big businesses. As a result, the procedures are more and the labor costs increase. The rewards obtained cannot be calculated. Therefore, when the company is recruiting, it should pay attention to big customers. It is worth having one more big customer and ten fewer small customers.

(9) The efficiency of canvassers It is undoubtedly necessary to pay attention to the efficiency of the staff. We have already described it in detail above. However, the personnel who go out to solicit business must also be given the same attention. However, internal personnel can be audited every day, while external personnel are not easy to deal with, because the whip is beyond reach and there is no way to check. However, we can estimate the efficiency of each person based on the achievements of each person, and decide to stay or leave. If the people you use are very efficient, then naturally. Why is the company's business so good?

(10) No business plan Business plan. Naturally, it is difficult to make money. For example, for Gu. If it is a car dealer, then. Test drive, contact, all kinds of procedures, there must be a predetermined plan. If it is a service company, then the customer must be reminded at that time for the purpose of repairing, refueling, etc., so as not to have their own business taken away by others. If the internal plan is set, everything can be carried out very smoothly.

(11) There are too many redundant staff The capital must be proportional to the size of the business scope. It has been mentioned slightly above. The problem of employment is also the same. If the affairs are cloudy, and many personnel are employed, it will certainly fail. Ordinary companies also like to arrange private individuals in the official office, so that efficiency cannot be obtained. Unnecessary consumption is enough to shorten the life of the company.

(12) Not researching why customers do not come Customers are the nurturers of the company's life. Their position should be highly valued in the company's eyes. In the eyes of shrewd operators, it is necessary to record the names and addresses of customers in detail, on the one hand to increase new customers, and on the other hand to maintain old customers. Once old customers do not come, they must immediately study the reasons for not coming in order to remedy them. If the company does not pay attention to these important events, how can it fail?

The reasons and remedies for business failure have been analyzed in great detail. At the moment when companies are preparing to expand their business in the New Year, I dare to offer these points with sincerity. Maybe it can help the business more or less.

Road Maintenance by Tan Wufei 252

The establishment of roads is originally intended to benefit transportation and facilitate merchants and travelers. Therefore, when it was first built, it was not unflat. However, after a long period of neglect, from light to heavy, the potholes became uneven. When the

At the beginning of the car's passage, it was not unstable. However, after a long period of traffic, from high to low, turning was uncomfortable. At this time, if we talk about maintenance, the cost will be huge and uneconomical. It is best to prevent the road construction team from organizing and dividing into two groups: road repair and road maintenance. If the road team manages several miles of road sections with a small number of workers, they should be on duty in sections and inspect them. If traces are found on the road surface, or if there is damage, fill it immediately to restore it to its original state. Until the road surface material can no longer be maintained, the road repair team will add materials and re-repair it to make it a complete road, and then carry out the road maintenance method. That's about it. In recent years, the construction of highways is too expensive to pour asphalt, and generally broken stone roads and sand and soil roads are the most common. Therefore, the maintenance methods are also different. According to the observations of the general public, the reasons for road damage can be summarized into two main points. One is weather damage, such as wind, rain, ice and frost, etc. One is mechanical damage, such as wheel rolling and hoof trampling. The speaker also said that 20% of the damage is caused by the weather, and 80% is caused by the machine wheels. This is only for the road surface. I said that or the declaration of war is poor, the roadbed is wet, or the roadbed is soft and sunken due to saturated moisture.

Page 29

That is also a major cause of damage to the public bombing. The maintenance method should adopt the patrol worker system. Patrol workers are long-term workers hired to specialize in road maintenance. They should be assigned to a designated road section, which is several miles long. There are several workers, led by the foreman. Inspect the road section under their jurisdiction every day. If there is any damage, level it according to the law immediately. Workers should patrol the road surface at least two people every day. This method is practiced in various countries and has achieved satisfactory results. Now, the maintenance methods for broken stone roads and sand and soil roads are described separately.

There are about eighteen items in the maintenance method of broken stone roads (1)

If the road surface is uneven, or there are ruts, and there is water storage, repair it with crushed stone to restore it to its original state. (2) The middle part of the road should always be higher than both sides, forming a shallow parabolic shape. (3) For roads with minor damage, dig up and repair them without adding crushed stone. (5) The excavated part of the road surface should be round and not be sharp-angled square corners. (5) The depth of excavation shall not be less than the maximum diameter of the stone block. (6) For roads with full excavation and repair, the middle part should be excavated first, and then both sides after repair. (7) Stone blocks shall not be discarded on the road surface. (8) Crushed stones that cannot pass through a one-and-a-half-inch sieve hole shall not be used. (9) The weight of each piece of crushed stone shall not exceed five taels. (10) Organic matter should be removed from the stone powder used as adhesive material. (11) The road surface should be watered frequently. (12) Rubbish, dregs, weeds and branches in ditches and culverts and under bridges should be cleaned frequently. (13) If there are small trees and deep grass at the road ends of culverts and bridges that hinder pedestrians and drivers' vision, they should be removed immediately. (14) Ditches with water accumulation should be dredged immediately. (15) Bridges, culverts, mileage signs, warning signs, highway huts, etc., should be repaired immediately if they are damaged. (16) Implement the collection of registration according to the rules for banning heavy vehicles. (17) Bridge wood beside the road.

There are about fourteen items in the maintenance method of sand and soil roads. (1) Road

Where the surface is uneven or ruts appear, use sand and soil to fill it up and compact it firmly to restore it to its original state. (2) The middle part of the road should always be higher than both sides, forming a parabolic green shape. (3) Stone blocks shall not be discarded on the road surface. (4) If the road letter softens after rain and becomes sticky, and mud adheres to the wheels, it is evidence of less sand. Use a pusher to level it immediately and spread a layer of sand. (5) If the road surface is dry on a sunny day and there is looseness, it is evidence of too much sand. Wait until after the rain, use a pusher to level it and spread a layer of soil. (6) When using a pusher, it must form a 45-degree angle with the center line of the road and scrape from the side of the road to the middle of the road. (7) The road surface should be watered. (8) The composition of the sand and soil used for patching the road should be the same as or made the same as the composition of the original road. (9) If there are rubbish, dregs, tree branches and weeds in ditches and culverts and under bridges, they should be cleaned frequently. (10) If there are small trees and deep grass at both ends of culverts and bridges that can hinder pedestrians and drivers' vision, they should be removed immediately. (11) Ditches with accumulated water should be dredged immediately. (12) Bridges, culverts, mileage signs, warning signs, highway huts, etc., should be repaired immediately if they are damaged. (13) Implement the ban according to the rules for banning heavy vehicles. (14) Protect roadside trees.

The above two methods of highway maintenance have been discussed in detail by the Construction Department of the Hebei Provincial Government. Now, I have added my own opinions for the attention of those who build highways in various places, so that they know that highways are not difficult to build at the beginning, but difficult to maintain after they are built, so as to be long-term and economical.

The Myriad Aspects of American National Highways by Xu Meilie 254

The smooth or blocked traffic is related to the prosperity or decline of the country. Entering its territory, if the fields are cultivated and the roads are well managed, then it is known that the country is strong and rich, and the culture is flourishing. Conversely, the country is poor and the people are weak, which can be known without asking. The roads are to the country as the meridians are to the body. When the meridians are open, the body is strong, and when the road network is dense, the country is prosperous. Those who observe the country do not need to seek and study deeply, and they can get a general idea of it. The United States, as a rising country in the New World, has dominated the world and become the richest of nations in less than two hundred years. Tracing back to the reason, although there are various main reasons, the development of transportation and the full exploitation of resources have contributed to it. The American road system is divided into national highways, state highways, county roads, and village roads. As far as national highways are concerned, the statistics of the forty-eight states show that the road lines are about 189,000 miles long, and about 78,000 miles have been improved and completed. The longitude and latitude are endless, densely woven like a net, and the transportation is convenient, ranking first in the world. Each year, the

The state allocates 75 million yuan for the construction of national highways. Now, President Hoover, in view of the fact that the roads in various states are very developed, but there is still a need for improvement and expansion, the original funding is insufficient, and the road budget must be increased. He has specially negotiated with the state governments on the economic cooperation plan. According to the report of the National Highway Administration, the mileage of road construction last year was shorter than in previous years. If the funding is not increased, the progress of all construction plans will not be as rapid as in the past few years. The reason why it was able to proceed according to the predetermined steps was due to the fact that the road construction fees in the early years had not been fully used, and the accumulated surplus over the years was very large. With this huge amount of money, the leap forward in road administration in the past few years could be promoted. Now, the savings have been exhausted, and the cost of labor and materials has also increased. It is not enough to rely on the annual funding alone. Therefore, the result is limited and reduced. If we want to seek rapid progress in roads, it will not be successful without increasing funding. Therefore, the central government has a plan to jointly raise road funds with the states. Now, most of the administrative heads of the states have agreed to assist as much as possible. However, the greatest driving force for the development of roads still depends on the central government. Regarding the specific movement to increase road funding, members of Congress have proposed a bill to increase the national highway annual fee to 125 million yuan. If it is approved, the trend of road administration in the future will be advancing rapidly again. According to the budget of the American Automobile Association, the national road and street construction and maintenance costs in 1930 will exceed 250 million yuan, and the number of workers needed will reach 625,000. If so, there will be even more amazing achievements in the world. It can be asserted. Investigation 255

The Business Status of Chinese Public Buses by Lin Yingmei

The China General Omnibus Company held its annual shareholders' meeting on February 25th at the General Manager's office in the Sassoon House. The meeting was chaired by Chairman Arnold (HEArnhold), who reported on the company's business status over the past year. The following is a translation of Mr. Arnold's speech:

Before reviewing last year's accounts, I have a few points to report to you, which I believe you will be pleased to hear. The rapid development of the company's business in the past year has been unprecedented. Southbound vehicles have been continuously added, and there are now as many as ninety-eight vehicles. Huge expansion plans are still actively underway. Once new vehicles are added to the fleet, the rush hour congestion can be dealt with. Adding vehicles to facilitate passengers and eliminate crowding is the company's consistent policy. In addition, running double-decker buses is another way to reduce congestion. Three have now been ordered for trial runs. The traffic congestion is similar to that of major cities around the world, which is not surprising. Transportation agencies, regardless of whether they are buses or trams, on the ground or underground, always have extra vehicles and personnel available for the comfort of passengers, so that there is no concern about congestion during rush hours. In that case, the huge daily expenses must be met by increasing fares. The company's vehicle mileage has increased by 60% compared to the previous year, so it is necessary to add maintenance equipment to cope with this. The original vehicle depot has been expanded, and a new office has been built at 263 Connaught Road, as the old buildings were no longer sufficient due to business development.

The public bus business cannot meet the needs of society without annual promotion and expansion. The new vehicles arriving in Shanghai this year still require further construction of buildings for protection. The company pays great attention to the maintenance of vehicles, and all employees are able to work diligently. Therefore, the number of vehicle breakdowns is comparable to that of well-known British companies when calculated by average mileage driven.

Breakdown Incidents

Unexpected breakdowns are a daily danger and concern in the transportation business, and are practically unavoidable. The company pays special attention to this to minimize breakdowns. Fortunately, with the concerted efforts of senior staff, considerable progress has been made in the past year. Last year, there were a total of 4,926 breakdown incidents (4,227 in the previous year), but most of them were minor accidents. All incidents, regardless of size, are recorded. The drivers employed by the company are all experienced, and some have been employed for two years without causing any accidents. The company's reward and punishment system is strict: awards are given for merit, and training is intensified for mistakes to reduce accidents and improve efficiency.

Labor Status

The company has not experienced any labor disputes of any nature in the past year. This is particularly worth reporting. In addition, the Chinese employee pension fund mentioned in last year's report has now accumulated to more than 23,000 taels. The relationship between the company and its employees is satisfactory. The company considers or accepts employee opinions, regardless of their position. All employees are diligent and competent, and follow the instructions of the board of directors and the general manager to develop the company's business. The degree of success can be seen in last year's profit and loss statement.

Accounting

Various accounting reports have been sent to you for several days, so I will not repeat them. Last year's net profit was 101,634.43 taels, as shown in the table, which I believe you have already seen. Adding the 13,838.54 taels carried over from the previous year, the total is 115,472.97 taels for distribution.

The directors propose to pay a dividend of 9% on the capital of one million taels, which requires deducting 90,000 taels. It is also proposed to transfer the balance of 71,294.85 taels under the "share premium" item to the "credit" and "expansion" items. A further 7,505.15 taels will be extracted from the "profit and loss" item to offset the above two items. The remaining balance of 17,967.82 taels in net profit will be carried over to the new accounts. The company's capital has increased from 703,000 taels to one million taels. The remaining 29,700 shares were all sold at a face value of ten taels, with an additional premium of two taels and five mace per share. As a result, the "share premium" item increased to 71,294.85 taels.

The vehicle and tire depreciation fund has also increased, and there seems to be no shortage. However, since the original vehicles were purchased, the exchange rate has suddenly plummeted, so the depreciation amount in the accounts is less than the replacement cost. The other star debtor accounts have been completely settled. The number of invoices issued is slightly higher than last year.

Assets

On the asset side, the credit item increased by 25,800 taels, of which 22,000 taels was paid to the original concessionaire. According to the contract, the concessionaire could purchase 10,000 shares of the company's stock at face value free of charge. Therefore, it is better to pay a lump sum to exchange for this option. The other item of 3,000 taels is the payment for receiving the branch road. Since the road was taken over, the business has been quite prosperous. The expansion account has not changed. It is now proposed to offset it together with the credit account, as mentioned above. The land account has not changed. The building account increased by 94,185.08 taels. The reason has just been explained. The total value of vehicles is 916,913.44 taels, all calculated at the actual price. The depreciation fund against this is 246,372 taels. Inventory increased to 111,634.43 taels. The other star

Page 30

All receipts, whose unpaid situations are not a cause for concern. The 147,058.89 taels owed by Arnhold & Co. is the company's floating balance, which is kept by the company in its capacity as a bank. In the future, it can be deducted from dividends or instructed to purchase new vehicles on behalf of the company. At the same time, this amount receives good interest income.

Business Overview 256

Various business statistics are dry and boring, and it is not possible to describe them in detail at this time. It is better to mention a few points briefly, which are more concise and clear. I believe you will be pleased to hear them. Last year, the company's vehicles traveled 3.5 million miles, carrying more than 33 million passengers, consuming 750,000 gallons of gasoline, and the fare income included 2,550 tons of copper coins. The length of tickets sold totaled 1,000 miles. Looking at everything, this industry has a bright future.

News 257

Recent News on the Shanghai-Jiading Long-Distance Bus Route 258

by Xiu Fan

Due to the muddy roads caused by the weather, the buses were suspended for nine days from the 7th. Normal service resumed on the 16th. News from the Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company: The Shanghai-Jiading bus route has been operating for several months since it opened. The number of passengers is high, and the business is very good. There are twelve round trips every day, all operating according to the published timetable. There have been no accidents involving missed or delayed departures. Travelers on the Shanghai-Jiading route generally praise this route. Due to excessive rainfall last winter and continuous spring rain in recent days for ten days without interruption, the newly built section of the road from Jiading to Luodian, which is fourteen Chinese miles long, has not been completed for long. The roadbed is not very firm, and has been repeatedly eroded by rainwater. The soil on the road surface has gradually become loose, and after being pressed by the heavy wheels of vehicles, it immediately presents an uneven surface with high and low points, and the soil is muddy and slippery, with accumulated water forming puddles, which is not good for travel. In order to avoid all dangers of overturning and injuring people, the company had no choice but to announce the suspension of service from the 7th. The weather has recently turned sunny and clear, and the soil is gradually drying. The road maintenance department is actively engaged in repairs, and the original condition can be restored soon. However, since the suspension of service has lasted for nearly ten days, the company felt that passengers would be inconvenienced if it was delayed further. Therefore, normal service resumed on the 16th.
